# üó∫Ô∏è World Lore

**World Setting: The Unfolding**  
**Campaign System:** Daggerheart (v1.5/1.6) **Theme:** Atlantis: The Lost Empire meets Magitek Steampunk. **Core Conflict:** Exploration vs. Stagnation.  
**I. The Cosmology: The Great Stitching**  
The world is not a static globe; it is a disjointed reality waiting to be pulled together.

* **The Magnetic Pull:** Nodes act as gravity wells for reality. When a new Node is claimed and harmonized, it physically pulls the new continent slowly toward the central Harmony continent. The world is literally being built/stitched together over time.  
* **The Threat (The Ether/Nether):** If civilization stops expanding, the reality of the claimed lands begins to dissolve. This has happened before, creating the "Dissolved Lands."  
* **The Crisis (The Minimum):** For centuries, Harmony has had excess power. Now, for the first time, they are approaching "The Minimum." If they dip below this threshold, Harmony tech (lights, trains, medical devices) will begin to lose charge.

**II. The Hub: Vumbua Academy ("The Safiri")**  
*Name subject to change based on language preference.*  
The Academy is the heart of **The Harmony**. It is a mobile city-state that teleports to the frontier.

* **The Current State:** The Academy has just transferred to a massive new Terra with 2 potential Nodes. However, early scans suggest these Nodes are "shattered" or weak. They are not the savior battery Harmony hoped for.  
* **The "Great Cull" Strategy:** Recognizing the desperation, the University has radically shifted its admissions policy.  
  * **Class Size:** The largest in history.  
  * **The Philosophy:** They expect 95% attrition during the "Trials" and another 20% loss during "Intern Voyages."  
  * **The Goal:** Stop training "Glory Seekers" and start manufacturing "Survivalists."  
* **Aesthetics:** High-Magitek. Brass, steam, crystal focusing lenses. But currently, the lights flicker occasionally‚Äîa secret terror for those who know why.

**III. The Explorer Castes**  
Harmony has two distinct types of explorers, often at odds:

1. **The Vanguard (The Front Runners):**  
   * **Role: They sail/ride off the edge of the map. They find where Nodes *likely* are.**  
   * **Vibe: Undisciplined, chaotic, glory-seeking. They rely on instinct. The map "unfurls" under their feet.**  
   * **Reputation: Rockstars, but unreliable.**  
2. **The Second Wave (The Grid-Makers):**  
   * **Role: They take the chaotic maps of the Vanguard and verify them. They ensure no Node was missed.**  
   * **Vibe: Methodical, scientific, disciplined.**  
   * **Reputation: The "Cleaners." They are currently being prioritized by the Academy because the Vanguard has missed things in their arrogance.**

**IV. The Factions**  
**1\. The Harmony (The New Empire)**

* **Philosophy:** Expansion is life.  
* **Strategic Paths:**  
  1. **Assimilation:** Convince found Clans to join Harmony (boosts Node efficiency).  
  2. **Discovery:** Find new Clans/Nodes in the Terra.  
  3. **The Unknown:** Go completely off the chart to find raw, unclaimed power.  
* **Harmony Tech:** Driven by "Crystal Batteries." These are links to the central network. They are designed to be power-capped to prevent overloads, but they are currently running lean.

**2\. The Remnants (The Failed Empire)**  
These Clans stagnated because they stayed "Natural" and "Low Tech." They adapted to their specific biome but failed to stitch the world together.

* **Clan Tech:** Non-existent. They use specialized, nature-based efficiency (e.g., bioluminescence instead of lightbulbs, beast-labor instead of engines). They are incredibly efficient at *one thing* but lack the versatility of Harmony.

**A. The Volcano Clan (The Pyre-Keepers)**

* **Status:** *Allied.*  
* **Biome:** Volcanic vents.  
* **The Node:** Heat/Fire.  
* **Motivations & Culture:**  
  * **The Contract of Blood:** They maintain a strict exchange of bloodlines to prevent corruption and inbreeding.  
  * **The Softening:** The Clan is physically thriving due to Harmony's medicine and food, but culturally, the elders fear they are becoming "soft." The Embers that used to require immense effort to heat a room now burn effortlessly with Harmony tech, making the youth complacent.  
  * **The Belief:** "Keep the Nodes warm with companionship." They view the fire as a living entity that requires social presence to survive.  
  * **The Fear:** If the world runs out of places to expand, the "Curse of Ash" will return, freezing their vents.

**B. The River Clan (The Wadi)**

* **Status:** *Hostile / Isolationist.*  
* **Biome:** The "Dry Vein" (Desert Canyon).  
* **The Node:** Water (Weak/Trickling).  
* **History:**  
  * **The Lost Bond:** They were once inextricably linked to the Air Clan. They lived *inside* the river walls, breathing via air bubbles provided by the Air Clan.  
  * **The Collapse:** When the Old Empire fell, the Air Clan retreated, the bubbles stopped, and the river dried up. The survivors were forced into the canyon floor.  
  * **Power Source:** They carry "Gems" that hold the residual environmental energy of their lost home.  
* **Natural Adaptation:** They have evolved to retain water like cacti. They wear "Still-Suits" made of organic leather to reclaim moisture.

**C. The Air Clan (The Renali)**

* **Status:** *Neutral / Elusive.*  
* **Biome:** The "Vapor Sea" (Floating Islands).  
* **The Node:** Wind/Gravity.  
* **Natural Adaptation:** They ride **Air-Bees** (Giant insects). They do not use engines; they use silk sails and insect pheromones to steer their islands.  
* **Secret Strength:** They are "accidentally strong" because their meandering path creates micro-connections with other distant Nodes, keeping their magic surprisingly potent.  
* **The "Bride Exchange" Ritual:**  
  * Strict orders are given: Do not see the ground, do not speak, do not merge crystals.  
  * Riders fly Air-Bees into the fog layer where visibility is zero.  
  * They drop a Clan member into the mist and blindly snatch a rope holding a person from a ground clan (or another island).  
  * This ensures genetic diversity without breaking their isolationist "flight" vow. The Air-Bees must *never* touch the ground.

**D. The Deep-Root Clan (The Mizizi) \[New Natural Concept\]**

* **Status:** *Unknown / Dormant.*  
* **Biome:** The "Petrified Forest" or "Fungal Deep."  
* **The Node:** Earth/Growth (Corrupted or Wild).  
* **Natural Adaptation:** They live inside the hollowed-out fossilized roots of ancient mega-flora. They use fungal spores for communication and defense. They are the "recyclers" of the world.

**V. Map Zones & Geography**

1. **The Vapor Sea:** The cloud layer separating the peaks. Requires airships or Air-Bees to cross.  
2. **The Dry Vein:** The desert canyon of the River Clan.  
3. **The Petrifaction Fields:** Where the Mizizi live. A forest turned to stone, now overgrown with massive fungi.  
4. **Tartannen:** The mythical "First City" of the old empire, rumored to be somewhere in this sector.

**VI. Player Hooks (The Intake)**

* **The Selection:** You are part of the massive intake. You are being tested not for your grades, but for your "Domain Resonance."  
* **The Stakes:** The Instructors are harsh. "Look to your left, look to your right. Both of them will likely be dismissed by noon."  
* **The Secret:** The Dean knows the power is failing. If this class doesn't find a strong Node, the lights at the Academy‚Äîand back home‚Äîwill go out forever.

# Bestiary

# **üìñ The Dual-Codex: Harmony vs. The Wilds**

**Concept:** The Academy views the frontier as a resource to be harvested. The Clans view it as a living entity to be negotiated with. **Mechanic:** Players can roll **Knowledge (Academic)** to get the Harmony entry, or **Knowledge (Culture/Nature)** to get the Clan entry. Usually, the Clan entry contains the *actual* solution to the encounter.

## **üêæ I. The Bestiary (Creatures of the Shattered Nodes)**

### **1\. The Ether-Jelly (Target of Prof. Ink)**

* **Visual:** A floating, translucent jellyfish the size of a cow, trailing neon-blue stingers that phase through solid matter.  
* **Harmony Classification:** *"Phase-Shift Cnidarian (Type 3 Pest)."*  
  * **The Science:** Non-sentient gas-bags. They clog intake valves and disrupt sonar. Protocol: Disperse with electric shock.  
* **Clan Lore (Trench-Kin / Iggy):** *"The Soul-Drifters."*  
  * **The Truth:** These are not animals; they are the memories of the land that has Dissolved. They are attracted to strong emotions.  
  * **Survival Tip:** Do not shock them; they explode into psychic static that wipes your memory. To move them, you must hum a low, sad tune. They will follow the vibration of grief.  
* **Recent Interaction:** Yesterday, a Copper-rank student tried to net one near the docks. He is now in the infirmary, physically fine, but he cannot remember his mother's name.

### **2\. The Void-Beast (Target of Cmdr. Blitz)**

* **Visual:** A sleek, six-legged predator made of shifting black smoke and obsidian teeth. It casts no shadow.  
* **Harmony Classification:** *"Aetheric Apex Predator (AAP)."*  
  * **The Science:** A carbon-based lifeform that hunts via thermal vision. Protocol: Overwhelming kinetic force and floodlights.  
* **Clan Lore (Ash-Blood / Ignatius):** *"Smoke-Stalkers."*  
  * **The Truth:** They do not hunt heat; they hunt *fear*. They are physical manifestations of the void trying to reclaim reality.  
  * **Survival Tip:** Running triggers their chase instinct. You must stand perfectly still and hold a "True Flame" (not Safe-Flame). They cannot cross a circle of real fire.  
* **Recent Interaction:** A patrol of "The Breakers" (Squad 02\) engaged a pack last night. They used floodlights. Two guards were dragged into the dark; their screams simply stopped instantly.

### **3\. The Rot-Shepherd (Mizizi Territory)**

* **Visual:** A hulking, shambling mound of compost, vines, and bones, shaped vaguely like a gorilla. It constantly sheds spores.  
* **Harmony Classification:** *"Parasitic Myco-Construct."*  
  * **The Science:** An animated accumulation of debris caused by wild spores. Invasive weed. Protocol: Incinerate immediately to prevent infection.  
* **Clan Lore (Mizizi / Britt & Aggie):** *" The Gardener."*  
  * **The Truth:** These are the immune system of the forest. They collect the dead to recycle them. They are peaceful unless you break a "Live Branch."  
  * **Survival Tip:** If you encounter one, bow and offer it "dead matter" (compost, old food, leather). It will trade you rare medicinal herbs for the "trash."  
* **Recent Interaction:** Dr. Rose Halloway (Squad 05\) burned a patch of "weeds" near the perimeter. A Rot-Shepherd retaliated by throwing a boulder through her lab window. Harmony calls it an "Unprovoked Attack."

### **4\. The Whispering Moth**

* **Visual:** A moth the size of a dinner plate with wings that look like blinking eyes.  
* **Harmony Classification:** *"Psionic Lepidoptera."*  
  * **The Science:** A hallucinogenic insect. Its dust causes temporary psychosis. Protocol: Wear filtration masks.  
* **Clan Lore (Universal):** *"The Liar-Bug."*  
  * **The Truth:** They mimic the voices of loved ones to lure travelers off cliffs.  
  * **Survival Tip:** If you hear your name called in the fog, cover your ears. If you answer, they steal your voice.  
* **Recent Interaction:** Lucky (Squad 09\) claims he heard his little sister calling from a ventilation shaft in the Deep-Hull. He was found clawing at a sealed grate, hallucinating that she was trapped inside.

## **üìú II. World Phenomena (The Physics of the Frontier)**

### **1\. "The Bleed" (Dissolution)**

* **Visual:** The edge of the map where the land turns into pixelated static and grey mist.  
* **Harmony View:** *"Dimensional Instability."*  
  * **Theory:** A lack of geometric scaffolding. The land is simply "falling off" the map.  
* **Clan View:** *"The Great Forgetting."*  
  * **Myth:** The world is a dream. When the dreamer wakes up, the edges fade.

### **2\. "The Minimum" (The Energy Crisis)**

* **Visual:** The flickering of the magitek lights; the groaning of the engines.  
* **Harmony View:** *"Temporary Efficiency Cycle."*  
  * **Propaganda:** We are re-routing power to the new expansion. It is a sign of growth\!  
* **Clan View:** *"Too Much Connection."*  
  * **Observation:** The City eats more than it bleeds. It is a parasite looking for a new host.  
  * **Secret Insight (Loami):** The boilers aren't just low on fuel; the *containment seals* are cracking. The city is trying to eat itself to stay alive.  
* **Recent Interaction:** The lights in the Copper Dorms (Block 99\) went out for 4 hours last night. Official reason: "Upgrades." Real reason: The Sky-Spire needed the juice for a dinner party.

### **3\. "Pre-Stitch" Artifacts (Ancient Tech)**

* **Visual:** Rusted, non-magical metal gears, combustion engines, and plastic found in the trash vortex.  
* **Harmony View:** *"Primitive Scrap."*  
  * **Theory:** Useless junk from civilizations that failed to achieve Harmony. Melt it down.  
* **Clan View (Earthkin/Mizizi):** *"The Old Iron."*  
  * **Myth:** Remnants of the "First Weavers" who built the world without magic.  
  * **Truth:** This tech doesn't require the Loom to function. It is immune to "The Minimum."  
* **Recent Interaction:** Old Man Silas found a "Combustion Generator" (a diesel engine). He got it running. It‚Äôs loud and smelly, but it *never flickers*. The Academy confiscated it as "Contraband."

## **üóùÔ∏è III. The Diplomatic "Truths"**

### **The Paper Men (The Envoys)**

* **Harmony History:** "Brave diplomats who peacefully negotiated the integration of the Clans."  
* **Clan History (Mizizi):** "Men in suits who smiled with their mouths but not their eyes. They signed the treaty in ink, but the paper smelled of ash."  
* **The Hook:** **Dean Vane** wears a ring identical to the one the Head Envoy wore when he burned the sacred grove to demonstrate "Safe-Flame."

### **The "Savant" Label**

* **Harmony Definition:** "A rare genetic anomaly allowing for high-performance magic."  
* **Clan Definition:** "Someone who hasn't been broken yet."  
* **The Hook:** The Academy treats Savants like prize racehorses. The Clans treat them like future martyrs.

### **The Exploranaut's Oath**

* **The Public Oath:** *"To seek the unknown and stitch it to the known."*  
* **The Whispered Oath (Among Veterans like Hesperus):** *"To survive the stupidity of command and bring the crew home."*

# Remnant Clans

# **Ancestral Knowledge & Academy Rumors**

*Confidential: Inherited beliefs based on Lineage in the era of "The Minimum".*

## **THE REMNANT CLANS (The Primal Elements)**

*Public Knowledge: There are FOUR known Remnant Clans: Ash-Bloods (New), Mizizi (New), Wadi (Dying), and Renali (First Contact era). Two others (Trench/Storm) are theoretically possible but currently unknown.*

### **5\. The Pyre-Keepers (Volcano Clan) [KNOWN / ACTIVE]**

* **The Element:** **MAGMA (Thermal Energy).**  
* **Rarity:** **Regional / Intense.**  
* **Node Intel:** **THE MAGMA HEART.**  
  * **The Physics:** The core heat of the planet. It creates land (rock) and destroys it.  
  * **The Value:** Industrial Heat. Harmony needs your temperatures to smelt their Iron and refine their Crystal. You are the "Kiln" of the empire.  
* **The Crisis:** **"The Cooling."**  
  * The vents are fading. The Elders fear the "Great Freeze" is coming.  
* **Ancestral Taboo:** **"The Obsidian Kiss."**  
  * *The Story:* A Fire-Prince once loved a River-Daughter. When they finally embraced, his heat met her water, and they instantly cooled into a single statue of screaming black glass. Mixing does not create life; it creates **Stasis**. Never touch the Water-Kin.  
* **View of the Academy:** **"The Great Furnace."**  
  * You were promised a city of eternal heat. You are disappointed to find it cold and sterile, but you stay because the "Crystal Batteries" feel like captured suns.  
* **First Contact Story:** **"The Beacon of Despair."**  
  * The Ash-Bloods realized their fires were dying. They deliberately created a massive smoke signal‚Äîa black pillar visible for miles‚Äîto *invite* Harmony. They traded their independence for heat.

    ### **6\. The Wadi (River Clan) [RARE / DECLINING]**

*Academy Status: Known but scarce. Their home node is fading, so few travel to the Academy.*

* **The Element:** **FRESH WATER (Hydrology).**  
* **Rarity:** **Scarce / Critical.**  
* **Node Intel:** **THE AQUIFER STONE.**  
  * **The Physics:** The solvent of life. It binds biological matter.  
  * **The Value:** Survival. You control a weak, trickling node, but because *everyone* needs water to live, you hold immense leverage. A cup of water in the desert is worth more than a ton of gold.  
* **The Crisis:** **"The Thirst."**  
  * The aquifers are empty. You lost your bond with the Air Clan long ago, and now you are dust-cacti people waiting for rain that never comes.  
* **Ancestral Taboo:** **"The Dry Grave."**  
  * *The Story:* A Water-Scout once fell asleep in a grove of the Root-Kin (Mizizi). The fungi did not attack him; they simply **drank**. He woke up as a desiccated husk, his moisture stolen to feed the rot. Never sleep near the green-bloods; they are always thirsty.  
* **View of the Academy:** **"The Iron Geyser."**  
  * You view the steam pipes and decorative fountains as a miracle and a sin. You are here to steal the secret of "Making Water" to save your canyon.  
* **First Contact Story:** **"The Stolen Water."**  
  * Strangers in metal suits walked into the Sacred Canyon. They carried canteens of sweet water but did not offer it. We thought they were mocking us. We took their moisture to survive. Then the "Paper-Man" (The Scrivener) came. He did not bring a weapon; he brought a contract. We signed it because he promised the water would flow again.

    ### **7\. The Renali (Air Clan) [RARE / REMOTE]**

*Academy Status: Known but elusive. They rarely land, making them a curiosity rather than a political force.*

* **The Element:** **WIND (Gas/Gravity).**  
* **Rarity:** **Abundant / Untamed.**  
* **Node Intel:** **THE SACRED WIND.**  
  * **The Physics:** Movement and mixture. Wind spreads seeds and regulates temperature.  
  * **The Value:** Transport. Harmony ships are heavy; they need your updrafts to save fuel. You control the "Highways" of the sky.  
* **The Crisis:** **"The Falling."**  
  * Your islands are drifting downward as gravity wins. The "Vapor Sea" is getting thinner.  
* **Ancestral Taboo:** **"The Heavy Heart."**  
  * *The Story:* A Rider who listened too long to the songs of the Volcano Clan found himself becoming "spiritually heavy." His Air-Bee refused to carry him. He didn't fall; he just sank. Never let the ground-dwellers anchor your mind.  
* **View of the Academy:** **"The Stone Cage."**  
  * It is heavy. It sits on the ground. It disgusts you. But you know the Academy has the "Lodestones" (Magnets) that could push your islands back up into the sky.  
* **First Contact Story:** **"The Caught Cloud."**  
  * The sky broke. A massive metal cloud (Harmony Airship) fell from the upper stream. It was heavy and dead, tumbling toward the ocean. We flew our Bees to catch it. We wove a net of silk and saved the metal-men. They were strange‚Äîthey did not know how to fly, only how to burn fuel to fight gravity. We pity them.

    ### **8\. The Mizizi (Deep-Root Clan) [KNOWN]**

* **The Element:** **BIOMASS (Carbon/Life).**  
* **Rarity:** **Common / Overgrown.**  
* **Node Intel:** **THE SPORE-MOTHER.**  
  * **The Physics:** The cycle of decay and regrowth.  
  * **The Value:** Medicine and Food. The Academy eats synthetic sludge; you offer real caloric density and healing compounds. You are the "Farm" and the "Hospital."  
* **The Crisis:** **"The Corrupted Growth."**  
  * The Petrified Forest is ancient, but it has stopped *decaying*. It is a cancer of eternal growth. Without decay, there is no new life. The cycle has stalled.  
* **Ancestral Taboo:** **"The White Scorch."**  
  * *The Story:* A Circle once allowed a Fire-Kin to warm their grove during a freeze. They woke to find their Ancestral Rot turned to sterile white ash. There were no spores left to carry the memory. Fire is not an element; it is an eraser.  
* **View of the Academy:** **"The Sterile Field."**  
  * Everything here is polished brass and glass. Nothing rots. It is terrifyingly clean. You are here to find the "Rot" (the entropy) that makes life possible.  
* **First Contact Story:** **"The Quarantine Breach."**  
  * The "Iron-Worms" (Bulldozers) ate the edge of the forest to lay a rail line. They released the "Corrupted Growth," which began infecting the workers. The Mizizi emerged not to fight, but to *quarantine* the mess. They joined Harmony only because they lacked the fire/chemicals to prune the corruption themselves.

    ## **THE HIDDEN CLANS (The Extreme Elements)**

*Elements pushed to their physical limit.*

### **9\. The Trench-Kin (The Abyssal) [UNKNOWN / SECRET]**

*Academy Status: Completely unknown. Even the Faculty doesn't know.*

* **The Element:** **TECTONIC PRESSURE (Deep Earth).**  
* **Rarity:** **Inaccessible.**  
* **Node Intel:** **THE SLEEPING GOD.**  
  * **The Physics:** The weight of the world. It stabilizes the continental plates.  
  * **The Value:** Stability. Without this Node, the continents would drift too fast and tear the rail lines apart.  
* **The Crisis:** **"The Bends."**  
  * The pressure in your caves is dropping. Your eyes are bulging; their blood is boiling. The weight of the ocean is lifting, and it is killing them.  
* **Ancestral Taboo:** **"The Surface Burn."**  
  * The light above burns the eyes. You wear heavy, fluid-filled goggles when topside to survive the "Vacuum" of surface pressure.  
* **First Contact Story:** **"The Deafening Whale."**  
  * We have never seen a "Human." But last cycle, a **"Deafening Metal Whale"** (Submarine) passed through the water above our cave. It did not swim like a beast; it hummed with a rhythm that hurt our ears. It dropped a glowing metal egg (probe) near our entrance. We buried it in sand because the light hurt our eyes.

    ### **10\. The Fulgur-Born (The Storm-Chasers) [RUMORED / ANOMALY]**

*Academy Status: Treated as a singular anomaly (Zephyr).*

* **The Element:** **PLASMA (Lightning).**  
* **Rarity:** **Volatile / Fleeting.**  
* **Node Intel:** **THE JUDGMENT SEAT.**  
  * **The Physics:** Pure, unshielded energy discharge.  
  * **The Value:** The "Jump Start." This Node is too dangerous to use for steady power, but it can kick-start a dead engine or overcharge a weapon in an emergency.  
* **The Crisis:** **"The Silence."**  
  * The storm is quieting. The lightning strikes are becoming infrequent. Without the strikes, your energy-based biology is starving.  
* **Ancestral Taboo:** **"The Grounding."**  
  * You never stand still. To stop moving is to lose your charge. You are constantly vibrating or pacing. Stasis is death.  
* **First Contact Story:** **"The Slow Walker."**  
  * A **"Slow-Walker"** (Vanguard Runner) entered the Glass Desert. He moved clumsily, dragging a metal sled. He had no charge‚Äîhe was dim. We skated to him to share the Spark, to "Judge" him. But he screamed and fired a weapon that threw a net. He fled before we could bless him with voltage. We learned that the Slow Ones fear the blessing.  
  * 

# Shattered Clans Lately

# **üìú The Diplomatic Dossier: State of the Frontier**

**Current Status:** Integration Phase (Year 2\) **Tension Level:** High / Philosophical Schism

## **üîó The Exchange: The Ritual of Separation**

For centuries, the Clans have remained isolated to prevent "The Shattering," but they recognized the need for genetic and cultural variance.

* **The Mechanism:** Every 5 years, the Clans meet at a neutral "Hollow Point" to exchange eligible adults in a marriage/integration ceremony.  
* **The Selection:** Only the most diligent, mature, and disciplined members are selected. They are vetted to ensure they have the willpower to keep the **Great Taboo**: Never speak of your home again.  
* **The Blind Journey:** To ensure isolation, the Clans maintain **no maps**. Only the Elders know the location and timing of the Exchange. The young are **blindfolded** from the moment they leave their village until they arrive at the Hollow Point, and again until they reach their new home. They literally do not know the path back.  
* **The Taboo:** Once exchanged, a member is considered **Dead** to their old clan. They are forbidden from speaking of their home traditions. To speak of the past is to invite the "Curiosity" that destroys worlds.  
* **The Exception (The Cloud-Kin):** The Storm Chasers (Fulgor-Born) are the only clan exempt from the blindness. They must move constantly to stay alive within the jet streams. Though they keep no physical maps, they cannot help but learn the land from above, witnessing the ruins of the empire they left behind. This makes them the most dangerous‚Äîand knowledgeable‚Äîof all the clans.  
* **The Current Cycle:** The last Exchange happened roughly 18 months ago, coinciding with Harmony's arrival. This means there is only **one** truly "new" exchange member (Zephyr) navigating this dual shock.

## **üçÑ I. The Mizizi (The Root-Kin)**

### **üèöÔ∏è The Tragedy: "The Burning Library"**

* **The Old Belief:** "When things stop dying, we start dying." The Mizizi believed they were trapped in a cycle of stagnation. They welcomed Harmony‚Äôs tools (solvents and shredders) to mulch the petrified forest, believing they were creating fertile soil for new life.  
* **The Horrifying Revelation:** **Senior Historian Nadine** and **Exploranaut Mosi** (the first Mizizi graduate) have discovered a terrifying truth in the lab. The petrified trees aren't just wood; they are **Data-Hardrives**.  
  * **The True History:** The Mizizi were not gardeners; they were the **Archivists of the Shattered Empire**. They were designed to be ever-living record keepers. The "Petrification" was a preservation method to save knowledge for the future.  
  * **The Interaction Protocol (The Tether):** Mizizi lore dictates they never connect to the Great Mother (the forest) alone. It is too vast. Prolonged connection causes "Strange Visions" (the Library attempting a data-dump).  
    * **The Method:** They work in pairs. One "Travels the Roots" (connects), and one "Anchors" (watches and pulls them back). They focus on each other to avoid being swept away by the archives.  
  * **The State of the Archive:** The library has been decaying for generations. The "New Growth" (non-decaying petrification) represents net-new storage or hardy fragments of the original Imperial Archive.  
  * **The Pruning (The Great Loss):** Tradition dictated pruning from **Oldest to Youngest**.  
    * **The Consequence:** They have been systematically deleting the ancient "Golden Age" history first.  
    * **The Remnant:** All that remains on the surface layers are the most recent recordings‚Äîtales of the Collapse, loss, and horror. These stories act as a terrifying "Gate," discouraging deep dives and reinforcing the belief that the past is pain. By destroying the deep roots, they are erasing the only proof that life was ever better.  
* **Harmony‚Äôs Stance:** "Stop the Mulch\!" Harmony is now desperately trying to convince the Mizizi Elders to *stop* destroying the trees. They want to preserve the history.  
* **Mizizi Elders‚Äô Stance:** "You promised us new life\!" They feel betrayed. They think Harmony wants to keep them trapped in the "Dead Stone" past instead of letting them grow.

### **üë• The "Foreign" Integers (Exchange Members)**

The Mizizi still participate in The Exchange, but their recent adoptees are reacting to Harmony in very different ways.

* **Zephyr (The Storm Voice):**  
  * **Origin:** **The Cloud-Kin (Storm Chasers).**  
  * **Public Status:** **"Foreign Dignitary" / Classified.**  
  * **The Outlier:** She arrived in the last exchange (18 months ago). Unlike the disciplined envoys of the past, the Storm-Kin are naturally wild and fearless. Most students assume she is an eccentric **Renali (Air Clan)** pilot, unaware she represents a completely different storm-based faction to the north. Only the Dean knows her true origin.  
  * **The Breach:** Zephyr breaks the Taboo not out of malice, but out of sheer, uncontainable excitement. She doesn't fear "The Shattering." She speaks openly of the "High-Jet Streams" and the "Thunder-Node."  
  * **Academy Relation:** Dean Vane has personally invited Zephyr into the inner circle. There are no spies here; the Dean and Zephyr can be found late at night in the Sky-Spire, eating sunflower seeds and frantically sketching wind-patterns on a chalkboard. Vane believes Zephyr holds the key to high-altitude flight.  
* **Rill (The River-Born):**  
  * **Origin:** **The Wadi (River Clan).**  
  * **Public Status:** **Mizizi Researcher.**  
  * **The Dilemma:** She arrived 6 years ago (previous cycle). She is deeply disciplined. While she doesn't hide her Wadi heritage, she focuses entirely on her work, making her seem like just another scholar.  
  * **The Conflict:** Her home Node is dying‚Äîa river reduced to a trickle. Her people sacrifice their own rainwater to feed the Node rather than drink it themselves. To see the Mizizi deliberately destroying their own "clan-blood" (the Forest) breaks her heart.  
  * **The Ruse:** She came to Vumbua last year claiming she wanted to study "Accelerated Decay" to help the Mizizi destroy the forest faster.  
  * **The Reality:** She is secretly researching to see if the forest *needs* to be destroyed at all. She is on the verge of a eureka moment regarding the forest's true nature, but she cannot act alone. She needs to find a Mizizi clan member to bring into the great discovery she has made.

### **üèõÔ∏è The Representatives**

* **Exploranaut Mosi (Council Member):** He is currently in a panic. He spends his days decoding the "Tree-Rings" of the logs scheduled for the furnace, trying to save fragments of history before they are burned. He is the bridge between Nadine's theory and his people's survival instinct.  
* **Kojo (Silver Student):** He works the Help Desk, trying to translate this new reality to incoming students. "We are not just roots," he tells them. "We are the scroll *and* the ink."

## **üî• II. The Ash-Bloods (The Ember-Kin)**

### **üåã The Resurgence: "The Conductive Theory"**

* **The Old Belief:** "The Cold Shoulder." Ash-blood history warns that outsiders are "Heat-Sinks"‚Äîparasites that steal warmth until the Obsidian turns grey and brittle. This is why they hid behind the Smoke Curtain.  
* **The Harmony Proof:** Since the Academy anchored near the ridge, the Obsidian Skin of the youth isn't fading‚Äîit is **brightening**.  
* **The Physics:** Harmony engineers proved that Ash-blood heat is exponentially amplified when in proximity to other active Nodes. They aren't batteries being drained; they are **Resonance Chambers** being rung.  
* **The Conflict:** The Elders remember the "Cold Times" and refuse to believe the data. The Youth (like Ignatius) feel the surge of power and want to rush toward the center of the city, terrifying their parents who think they will burn out.

### **üíî The Broken Exchange**

* **The Event:** This year, the Ash-Bloods were scheduled to send a bride to the **Trench-Kin**.  
* **The Decision:** They didn't show up. With their volcanoes reignited by Harmony, they no longer feel the need to trade for "New Blood" to survive. They believe they have ascended beyond the old ways.  
* **The Insult:** Instead of a person, they dropped a **Obsidian Tablet** down the exchange shaft. It read: *"The Heat has returned. We need nothing from the Dark. Look to the Light."*

### **‚öñÔ∏è The Trade Agreement (The Boiler Room Pact)**

* **Status:** Enthusiastic Partnership (among the youth).  
* **The Reality:** Ash-bloods aren't forced into the boilers; they beg for the shifts. The Boiler Room is the only place in Vumbua hot enough to feel like "Home" without the stifling containment suits.  
* **The Innovation:** Rather than using generic "Potential Energy" cores, Harmony has retrofitted the entire port engine to run on **Direct Obsidian Transfer**. It is 300% more efficient, and the Ash-bloods take immense pride in being the literal heartbeat of the city.

### **üèõÔ∏è The Representatives**

* **Lady Ignis:** She is not a hostage; she has traveled to **Harmony Seat** to join the High Council as the Representative of the Clans.  
  * **The Power:** In accordance with Harmony's "Inverse Power Doctrine" (the belief that the newest among them should hold the most power), she was granted tremendous voting weight. She instantly became one of the most important figures in the land, creating laws for a society she barely understands but holding massive sway over new Frontier charters.  
  * **The Act:** It was *her* signature on the "Expansion Bill" that authorized the relocation of Vumbua Academy to the Ash-blood Isles.  
  * **The Retinue:** She attempted to bring the Mizizi Elders to the capital, but they refused. Instead, she traveled with the majority of the Ash-blood Elders (those fit for travel) and was escorted by **Captain Elara Thorne** (the exploranaut who first contacted her people), who has only just returned to Vumbua to assist with the intake.  
  * **The Belief:** She believes that political integration at the highest level is the only way to ensure her people are partners, not fuel.

## **üï≥Ô∏è III. The Earthkin / Trench-Kin (The Deep Dwellers)**

### **ü§ù The Discovery: Iggy's Secret**

* **The Cover-Up:** When the Ash-Bloods dropped the Obsidian Tablet ("Look to the Light"), the Trench-Kin Elders were terrified. They buried the tablet, fearing that curiosity about the "Light" would destroy their society.  
* **Iggy's Origin:** **Iggy** was a deep-tunnel scrapper who found the buried tablet. He didn't read it as an insult; he read it as an invitation.  
* **The Motivation:** He isn't on the surface to conquer; he is here to find out why the Ash-Bloods stopped coming. He suspects the surface isn't a "Burning Hellscape" (as the Elders teach) but a place of infinite energy.

### **üèõÔ∏è The Representatives**

* **Status:** **HIDDEN / UNCONTACTED.** Harmony has no official contact with the Trench-Kin. The Academy believes the deep crust is composed of lifeless rock and pressurized gas pockets. They have no idea a civilization exists below.  
* **Iggy (Gold):** He is not a diplomat; he is an **Unregistered Infiltrator**. He passed the entrance exams by simply not listing a home address and letting the registrars assume he was a generic "Earth-Elemental" construct or mutation. He represents the potential of a people who have not yet introduced themselves.

## **üîç IV. The Shattered Empire Theory (The Research)**

**The Project:** "The Unification Hypothesis" **Lead Researchers:** **Dean Isolde Vane** (The Architect) & **Senior Historian Nadine** (The Theorist).

* **The Theory:** The Clans (Mizizi, Ash-blood, Trench-kin, and the rumored Cloud-kin) are not separate species. They are **specialized castes** of a single, global civilization that shattered 10,000 years ago.  
  * **Mizizi:** The Archivists (Memory).  
  * **Ash-bloods:** The Engines (Power).  
  * **Trench-kin:** The Miners (Resources).  
  * **Cloud-Kin:** The Architects (Vision).  
  * **Harmony:** The Navigators (Direction).  
* **The Implication:** They were *designed* to function together. The "Disaster" the clans fear wasn't caused by proximity; it was caused by **separation**. The machine broke, and the parts drifted away.  
* **The Goal:** To prove to the isolationist Elders that "The Great Stitching" isn't a new empire conquering them‚Äîit is a **Repair Mission**.

## **üî¨ V. Dean Isolde Vane (The Heimerdinger Archetype)**

* **Vibe:** A small, bustling ball of intellect and empathy. Think Heimerdinger (Arcane). She is brilliant, scattered, and deeply caring.  
* **The Office:** A chaos of floating chalkboards, half-finished prototypes, and cups of cold tea.  
* **The Motivation:** She isn't a politician; she is a problem solver. She views the Clans not as "subjects" but as "lost family members."  
* **Relationship with Zephyr:** She is fascinated by Zephyr. She treats her like a granddaughter and a fellow scholar, spending hours asking about wind currents. There is no manipulation here‚Äîjust pure, unadulterated scientific joy.  
* **Quote:** *"Don't you see, Mosi? The Ash-bloods are the fuel, the Mizizi are the memory, and we are the steering wheel\! We aren't building a city‚Äîwe're putting the giant back together\!"*

# Lore Update

# **üìñ The Vumbua World Bible**

**Setting:** A "Magitek-Steampunk" reality defined by The Great Stitching. **Aesthetic:** 1920s Oxford meets *Treasure Planet*. Brass, teal energy, stone masonry, and modular construction.

## **üèóÔ∏è I. The Architecture of the Academy**

Vumbua is not a vehicle; it is a **Mobile Modular City**.

### **The 30/70 Rule**

* **The Cores (30%):** These are the only permanent, moving structures. They teleport/fly to new frontiers and act as the anchors.  
  * **The Sky-Spire:** A vertical, golden airship (Command, Elite Dorms, Navigation).  
  * **The Deep-Hull:** A massive iron steamship (Classrooms, Logistics, Mess Halls).  
  * **The Walker-Core:** A four-legged industrial power unit \- on the edge of the proper grounds, It and the ship can transport each other (slowly) (Engineering, Power, The Loom).  
* **The Spire-Scape (70%):** Upon landing, thousands of "Worker-Constructs" swarm out to assemble a temporary city around the Cores.  
  * **Visuals:** A forest of scaffolding, steam cranes lifting prefab dorms, and ley-lines being laid directly into the dirt. It feels like a high-tech refugee camp mixed with a World's Fair.

## **üîÆ II. Magic & Technology ("Harmony")**

### **Geometric vs. Wild Magic**

* **Harmony (Geometric):** The Academy‚Äôs magic is rigid, formulaic, and "Safe." It uses tuning forks, crystals, and math to impose order on chaos.  
  * *Visual:* Teal, steady, geometric shapes. Quiet hums.  
  * *Example:* **"Safe-Flame"** (Chemically stabilized fire that provides heat without burning wood).  
* **Variance (Wild):** The magic of the Clans (Ash-blood, Mizizi, Earthkin). It is raw, emotional, and unpredictable.  
  * *Visual:* Orange/Green/Brown, flickering, organic shapes. Crackling or singing sounds.  
  * *Example:* **"True Spark"** (Ignatius‚Äôs fire that consumes oxygen and casts dancing shadows).

### **The "Loom" & Bureaucracy**

* **The Loom:** A massive crystal computer in the Walker-Core. It calculates probabilities and assigns ranks.  
* **The Receipt:** The *only* official proof of status. A narrow strip of parchment printed by 1920s-style typewriters. Without a receipt, you are a non-entity.  
* **Resource Currency:** "Charge" or "Battery Hours." Gold is decorative; energy is survival.

## **üìú III. History & Politics**

### **The "Silent Era" (80 Years Ago \- Present)**

* **The Drought:** For eight decades, no new Nodes were found. Maps remained static. The culture of exploration stagnated into academic theory.  
* **The Consequence:** "Exploranauts" became celebrities/myths rather than active agents. The Academy became stuffy and elitist.  
* **The Awakening:** The discovery of the new Terra (Mizizi/Ash-blood lands) has shattered the silence. The city is in a "Gold Rush" frenzy.

### **The "Minimum" (State Secret)**

* **The Truth:** Harmony is running out of power. The "Silent Era" drained the batteries.  
* **The Lie:** The Dean claims the new expansion is for "Glory" and "Destiny."  
* **The Stakes:** If the Venture fails, the Academy cannot travel back. They will be stranded without enough power to travel Vumbuas cores. 

## **üåø IV. The Integrated Clans**

### **The Mizizi (The Root-Kin)**

* **Origin:** The Petrified Forest (Deep Frontier).  
* **The Hook:** Their Node contains a resonance that **halts decay**.  
* **Academy View:** "A medical miracle waiting to be harvested."  
* **Clan View:** "When things stop dying, we start dying." (They need the cycle of rot to survive).  
* **Stereotype:** Slow, fungal, weird. "Gardeners."

### **The Ash-Bloods (The Ember-Kin)**

* **Origin:** The Volcanic Ridges.  
* **The Hook:** Their Node pulses with **Primal Heat** (infinite geothermal energy).  
* **Academy View:** "A new battery for the forges."  
* **Clan View:** Fire is a living ancestor, not a fuel source.  
* **Stereotype:** Volatile, dangerous, "Savages" who refuse to use Safe-Flame.

## **‚öîÔ∏è V. Hierarchy & The "Rust" Reality**

### **The Ranks**

1. **Gold (Aurum):** The Aristocracy. 1% of students. Too expensive to fail (demoted to Copper, never Rust).  
2. **Silver (Argent):** The Professionals. 24% of students. The actual workforce.  
3. **Copper (Aes):** The Bulk. 55% of students. Laborers and grunts.  
4. **Rust (Ferrum):** The Culled. 20% of students.  
   * *Fate:* They are stripped of their receipts and reassigned to "City Maintenance" (sewers, scrap-haulers) or **Squad 09** (Trap Detection). They are effectively non-citizens.

### **The "Savant" Loophole**

The Loom is programmed to identify **"High-Variance"** (Outliers).

* A Copper/Silver student who solves a problem using "Wild Magic" (unsanctioned methods) can trigger a "Savant" flag.  
* *Risk:* High. It can lead to promotion (Gold) or branding as a Heretic (Expulsion).

# Integration

# **‚è≥ The Vumbua Timeline: 3,000 Years of The Stitching**

**Core Philosophy:** "We do not conquer land; we wake it up." **The Mechanic of Integration:** Symbiotic Resonance.

## **‚ö° Part I: The Mechanics of Integration (How it Works)**

Every Node is a dormant battery of a specific type of reality (Heat, Growth, Light, Gravity).

* **The Dormant State:** Isolated Nodes are weak. Their power is local and inefficient (e.g., Ash-blood lava only heats the mountain; Mizizi forests grow slowly).  
* **The Spark (Symbiosis):** Integration requires a **Two-Way Flow**.  
  1. **Inward Flow:** The raw material of the new Node (Obsidian) is used to power Harmony tech (Boilers) at 100% efficiency.  
  2. **Outward Flow:** Harmony's "General Battery" (Geometric Potential) is used in the new territory to power a local function (a camp stove) at lower efficiency.  
* **The "Click":** When both flows happen simultaneously, the realities lock together. The new land physically lurches toward Harmony. The power amplifies exponentially.

### **üö´ The Mizizi Failure (Why they aren't integrated)**

* **The Block:** Harmony has failed to establish the **Outward Flow**.  
  * They tried to bring "New Life" (Solvents/Fertilizer), but the Forest rejected it as poison.  
  * **The Missing Key:** Harmony has not yet brought **"Stored Knowledge"** (Books/Data) into the forest.  
  * **The Theory:** The Mizizi Node is "The Memory." It doesn't eat fertilizer; it eats *history*. Until Harmony physically carts their Archives into the Petrified Forest, the circuit will remain open, and the Mizizi will remain "Diluted."  
  * **The Reciprocal Lock:** Additionally, the connection remains blocked until Mizizi bark is used to create paper‚Äîtransforming their physical form into a vessel for knowledge‚Äîwithin the proximity of an integrated Core (which the Ash-blood Volcanoes now count as).

## **üìú Part II: The Historical Timeline**

### **Era 1: The First Spark (3,000 Years Ago)**

* **The Event:** Two primitive tribes‚Äî**The Weavers** (Constructors) and **The Navigators** (Star-Readers)‚Äîmeet on a dying shard of reality.  
* **The First Stitch:** Instead of fighting for the last scraps of food, a Weaver uses a Navigator's star-chart to power a loom. The realities fuse. The land stabilizes.  
* **The Result:** The founding of **Harmony Prime**. The first city is born.

### **Era 2: The Resource Wars (2,500 \- 1,500 Years Ago)**

* **The Conflict:** As Harmony expanded, they encountered **The Iron-Clad** (Metal-Kin) and **The Tide-Callers** (Water-Kin).  
* **The War:** Harmony tried to *conquer* the Nodes instead of harmonizing them.  
* **The Consequence:** The "Dissolved Lands." Entire continents shattered because the energy flow was one-way (extraction only).  
* **The Lesson:** "You cannot steal a Node; you must marry it."

### **Era 3: The Golden Stitch (1,500 \- 1,000 Years Ago)**

* **The Peace:** Harmony adopts the "Inverse Power Doctrine." The newest/weakest members are given the most political power to ensure fair Symbiosis.  
* **The Expansion:** A massive boom. The Wind-Kin, the Glass-Walkers, and the Crystal-Singers are integrated. Harmony becomes a continent.  
* **The Tech:** The first "Teleporting City" (Vumbua) is built to hunt for distant Nodes.

### **Era 4: The Long Lull (1,000 Years Ago \- 80 Years Ago)**

* **The Stagnation:** New Nodes become harder to find. The distances grow vast.  
* **The Shift:** Vumbua becomes an academic institution rather than an explorer's guild. "Exploranaut" becomes a title for historians, not adventurers.  
* **The Decay:** Without new Resonance, the batteries slowly begin to drain. The edges of Harmony start to fray (The Bleed).

### **Era 5: The Silent Era (80 Years Ago \- Present)**

* **The Drought:** Not a single Node is found for three generations.  
* **The Crisis:** "The Minimum." The lights flicker. The Council panics but keeps it secret.  
* **The Discovery (2 Years Ago):** A desperate deep-scan reveals two faint pulses in the "Shattered Sector"‚ÄîThe Ash-bloods (Heat) and the Mizizi (Memory).  
* **The Rush:** Vumbua teleports for the first time in a century.

## **üåç Part III: The "Shattered Node" Ecology**

Every Node creates a unique civilization (Biome) around it. It isn't always human.

### **1\. The Obsidian Ridges (Ash-Blood)**

* **The Biome:** Volcanic glass and magma.  
* **The Civ:** Humanoid/Elemental hybrids.  
* **Integration Status:** **100%.**  
  * *Inward:* Obsidian powers the Boilers.  
  * *Outward:* Harmony batteries power their cooling suits.  
  * *Result:* The volcanoes are roaring. The Ash-bloods are thriving.

### **2\. The Petrified Forest (Mizizi)**

* **The Biome:** Massive, stone-flesh trees that "breathe" dust.  
* **The Civ:** Fungal-Turtle hybrids (Mizizi).  
* **Integration Status:** **15% (Stalled).**  
  * *Inward:* Soil powers the Hydroponics (Weak connection).  
  * *Outward:* Harmony Solvents kill the trees (Rejection).  
  * *Result:* The forest is dying, but the Node isn't waking up.

### **3\. The Abyssal Trench (Trench-Kin)**

* **The Biome:** High-pressure underwater vents.  
* **The Civ:** Earth/Crab hybrids.  
* **Integration Status:** **0% (Hidden).**  
  * *Potential:* Harmony pumps could aerate their water; Trench-crystals could harden Harmony hulls.

### **4\. The Cloud-Vaults (Storm Chasers)**

* **The Biome:** Solidified lightning clouds in the jet stream.  
* **The Civ:** Avian/Energy beings (Rumored).  
* **Integration Status:** **Unknown.**  
  * *Potential:* Infinite electrical power vs. Weather control tech.

# Harmony Factions

# **üèõÔ∏è The Harmony Factions: Pillars of the Empire**

**Context:** The Empire of Harmony is governed by families who control specific elemental physics. **The Political Divide:**

* **The Venture Council (The Core Four):** The expeditionary forces running Vumbua Academy. They are focused on **Exploration & Survival**.  
* **The Domestic Council (The Civilian Pillars):** The powers running the static capital, Harmony Prime. They are focused on **Stability & Exploitation**.

## **üöÄ I. The Venture Pillars (The Core Four)**

*These factions dominate the Academy. They are the "Flight Crew" of the mobile city.*

### **üíé 1\. House Gilded (The Highborne)**

* **Sphere:** Capital, Energy Storage, Investment.  
* **The Element:** **PURE CRYSTAL (The Battery).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"Assimilation is Profit."*  
* **History:** Rose to power in **Era 1** by perfecting the storage of raw magic, allowing civilization to exist at night.  
* **The "Minimum" Motive:** The Crystal Banks are insolvent. They need the **"Great Surge"** (500 years of power) not just to keep the lights on, but to hide the fact that they leveraged the empire's future on bad energy bets during the Silent Era.  
* **Key NPCs:**  
  * **Valerius Sterling (Captain/Student):** Represents the arrogant youth who believes the world owes him a legacy.  
  * **Lady Vespera (Captain):** Represents the ruthlessness of Highborne trade.

### **üõ°Ô∏è 2\. The Vane Lineage (The Orderborne)**

* **Sphere:** Defense, Walls, Reality Anchors.  
* **The Element:** **COLD IRON (Magnetism).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"Defense is Survival."*  
* **History:** Gained dominance during the **Resource Wars (Era 2\)** when the borders destabilized. They built the walls that kept the monsters out.  
* **The "Minimum" Motive:** They know the "Perimeter" is failing. The Ether Beasts are evolving. They view the "Shattered Circuit" not as a puzzle, but as a breach in the wall. They want to **force** the circuit closed to re-arm the shields.  
* **Key NPCs:**  
  * **Lord Commander Titus Vane:** The militant rival to the Dean. He believes the Academy is too soft and scientific. He pushes for aggressive exploration ("Find and Secure") rather than empathetic understanding. He views the Clans as strategic assets to be conscripted.  
  * **Celia Vance (Proctor):** The rigid enforcer of safety protocols.  
  * **Kaelo "Ghost" Vane (Captain):** The black-ops wing of the family.

### **üìú 3\. The Scrivener Guild (The Loreborne)**

* **Sphere:** Navigation, Maps, Data, History.  
* **The Element:** **AETHER (Data/Echoes).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"Discovery is Truth."*  
* **History:** Descendants of the original **Navigators** (Era 1). They decoded the laws of "Symbiotic Resonance" in **Era 3**.  
* **The "Minimum" Motive:** They are the keepers of the **"Dark Ages" Secret**. They know the Empire collapsed once before due to isolation. They are terrified that the Mizizi are burning the archives because the Mizizi trees contain the *only* record of exactly *how* the previous collapse happened.  
* **Key NPCs:**  
  * **Dean Isolde (The Architect):** The Head of the Academy. A brilliant, Heimerdinger-esque savant who views the Stitching as a complex equation of empathy and physics. She is desperate to solve the puzzle before the lights go out, but refuses to use the brute force methods of the Vanes.  
  * **Professor Ink (Captain):** Represents the pure thirst for knowledge.  
  * **Senior Historian Nadine:** Working with the Dean to prove the "Shattered Empire" theory.

### **‚öôÔ∏è 4\. The Iron-Union (The Ridgeborne)**

* **Sphere:** Engines, Labor, Industry, Heat.  
* **The Element:** **STEAM (Pressure/Force).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"Stabilization is Duty."*  
* **History:** Split from the original **Weavers** in **Era 2**. While the Architects focused on static stone, the Union focused on *machines*. They are the Blue-Collar nobility.  
* **The "Minimum" Motive:** They are the only ones who physically feel the "Ghost Charge." They are pushing hardest for **Ash-blood Integration** because the Obsidian direct-transfer is the only thing keeping the boilers from exploding.  
* **Key NPCs:**  
  * **Loami (PC):** The prodigy mechanic.  
  * **"Old Man" Silas (Captain):** The cynical veteran who knows where the bodies are buried.  
  * **"Hammer" (Squad 05 Leader):** The ambitious climber.

## **üèõÔ∏è II. The Civilian Pillars (The Domestic Auditors)**

*These factions have just arrived in Vumbua's wake. They view the Academy as a reckless expense and want to strip-mine the frontier.*

### **üåæ 5\. The Verdant Trust (The Agri-Lords)**

* **Sphere:** Agriculture, Food, Biology.  
* **The Element:** **HUMUS (Carbon/Growth).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"Growth is Mandatory."*  
* **The Crisis:** The topsoil in Harmony Prime is dead. The Empire is 6 months away from famine.  
* **Agenda in Vumbua:** They want to seize the **Mizizi Forest**. They don't care about the "Memory Node" or the history; they see millions of tons of fertile compost. They are lobbying to **mulch the entire forest** immediately to send fertilizer back home.  
* **Conflict:** They are the natural enemies of the Mizizi and the Scriveners (who want to save the trees).  
* **Key Agent:** **Overseer Grimaldi.** A massive man in a green velvet suit offering huge bounties for "Life-Soil."

### **‚öñÔ∏è 6\. The High-Justiciars (The Scales)**

* **Sphere:** Law, Contracts, Political Balance.  
* **The Element:** **LEAD (Weight/Finality).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"The Balance Must Hold."*  
* **History:** Formed in **Era 3** to enforce the "Inverse Power Doctrine." They ensure new Nodes get political power to prevent the Core Families from becoming tyrants.  
* **Agenda in Vumbua:** **The Audit.** They believe Dean Vane is cooking the books regarding the energy output. They are investigating why the Ash-blood and Mizizi nodes are under-performing (The Shattered Circuit leak). They threaten to shut down the Academy if the numbers don't balance.  
* **Key Agent:** **Adjudicator Kael.** A woman in a lead-lined coat who follows Dean Vane's staff, demanding un-redacted logs.

### **üß± 7\. The Grand Architects (House Mason)**

* **Sphere:** Construction, Cities, Housing.  
* **The Element:** **GRANITE (Permanence).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"Stone Remembers."*  
* **History:** The other half of the original **Weavers**. They despise the Iron-Union's "temporary" metal machines. They build for eternity.  
* **Agenda in Vumbua:** They hate the "Modular City" aesthetic of Vumbua. They want to pave the Ash-blood Isles and build a static stone fortress. They are trying to evict the Mizizi from their "unsafe" cliffside dorms.  
* **Key Agent:** **Architect Stone.** A dwarf with geomantic granite hands who is trying to condemn Block 04-Root.

### **‚öì 8\. The Syndicate of Sails (The Logistics)**

* **Sphere:** Trade, Transport, Currency Flow.  
* **The Element:** **MERCURY (Fluidity).**  
* **Philosophy:** *"Momentum is Value."*  
* **History:** Privatized Quartermasters from the Silent Era. They control the flow of goods between Nodes.  
* **Agenda in Vumbua:** **Monopoly.** They know the **Storm Chasers (Cloud-Kin)** control the jet streams. They want to find them *first* to secure exclusive trade rights to the high-altitude routes.  
* **Key Agent:** **Broker Silas.** A slick fixer in the Celestial Lounge trying to buy the loyalty of Rust-tier students (like Lucky) to map the black market routes.

# Harmony Timeline

# **‚è≥ The Vumbua Timeline: 3,000 Years of Harmony**

**Core Philosophy:** "Unity is Physics." **The Mechanic:** The Great Stitching is not magic; it is a circuit.

## **‚ö° Part I: The Mechanics of Integration (Symbiotic Resonance)**

Integration is the process of locking two disparate realities into a single flow. It requires a simultaneous, two-way energy exchange.

### **1\. The Inward Flow (The Raw to the Refined)**

* **Action:** The raw material of the new Node must be used to power an integrated technology at **100% efficiency** within the radius of an already Integrated Core.  
* **Example (Ash-Bloods):** Raw Obsidian taken from the ridge is placed into a Harmony Boiler. It burns hotter than coal. The energy creates a "Tether" back to the source.

### **2\. The Outward Flow (The Refined to the Raw)**

* **Action:** A Harmony "Battery" (Geometric Potential) must be used within the territory of the new Node to power a local necessity, proving that Harmony sustains the new land.  
* **Example (Ash-Bloods):** A Harmony battery is used to power a cook-stove or cooling suit inside the volcano. The local reality accepts the foreign energy.

### **3\. The Lock (The Stitch)**

* When both flows occur, the "Safe Lane" opens. The Aether-beasts are pushed back by the resonance, creating a stable travel corridor. The Nodes pull toward each other ever so slowly (hundreds of years to move a mile)

### **üö´ The Mizizi Blockage (The Current Puzzle)**

The Mizizi are stalled because the circuit is incomplete. The purpose of the forest is not yet understood making it impossible to perform the integration

* **Inward Failure:** Harmony has not yet taken Mizizi Bark, turned it into paper, and filled it with knowledge near an Integrated Core (The Ash-Blood Volcanoes).  
* **Outward Failure:** Harmony tried to bring "Fertilizer" (Growth) to the forest. But the Mizizi Node is **Memory**, not Biology. To create the Outward Flow, Harmony must cart **Stored Knowledge** (Books/Archives) into the forest to "feed" the trees.

## **üìú Part II: The Harmony History (3,000 \- 1,000 Years Ago)**

### **Era 1: The First Spark (3,000 Years Ago)**

* **The Origin:** Two warring tribes‚Äî**The Weavers** (Constructors) and **The Navigators** (Star-Readers)‚Äîmet on a dying shard of reality surrounded by Aether Beasts.  
* **The Unification:** Instead of fighting, a Weaver used a Navigator's star-chart to power a loom. The realities fused. **Harmony Prime** was born.  
* **The Core Families Emerge:**  
  * **House Gilded** perfected the Crystal Battery to store the spark.  
  * **The Iron-Union** built the engines to utilize it.

### **Era 2: The Resource Wars (2,500 \- 1,500 Years Ago)**

* **The Conflict:** Harmony expanded aggressively. They tried to extract resources without completing the "Outward Flow."  
* **The Consequence:** The **Vane Lineage** (Defenders) rose to power during this era, building the walls to keep the Aether Beasts out as the borders destabilized.  
* **The Lesson:** "One-way flow leads to Dissolution."

### **Era 3: The Golden Stitch (1,500 \- 1,000 Years Ago)**

* **The Discovery:** The **Scrivener Guild** decoded the "Symbiotic Resonance" laws.  
* **The Boom:** A golden age of integration. Several "Great Nodes" (sentient civilizations) were found and stitched. The continent grew massive.  
* **The Peace:** For a millennium, there was no major war. Just quiet periods of consolidation followed by the excitement of a new Stitch.

## **üåä Part III: The Long Silence (1,000 Years Ago \- Present)**

### **Era 4: The Dwindling (1,000 \- 80 Years Ago)**

* **The Shift:** The Great Nodes (Sentient Civs) were all found. Explorers began finding only "Minor Nodes"‚Äîislands of pure biology (giant insects, sentient plants, elemental pockets).  
* **The Sustainment:** These Minor Nodes kept the lights on, but they didn't expand the culture. Harmony entered a period of comfortable stagnation.  
* **The Logistics:** To integrate a Node, a crew had to stay behind to maintain the "Outward Flow" battery. Being an Exploranaut meant saying goodbye forever to hold the door open for the rest of civilization.

### **Era 5: The Silent Era (80 Years Ago \- Present)**

* **The Crisis:** The Minor Nodes dried up. The Ocean of Aether became impassable. Monsters crowded the shores, locking Harmony onto its continent.  
* **The Bravery of the Vanes:** With no guarantee of return, **Captain Elara Thorne** and **Valerius Sterling Sr.** led suicide missions into the blind mist. They mapped the currents by hand, losing ships and crew to finding *nothing*.  
* **The "Minimum":** While the general populace rested on their laurels, believing their power infinite, the Council saw the reserves dwindling. The batteries weren't critical yet, but the trend line was terrifying. To combat public apathy without causing panic, the Council began offering staggering rewards for exploration. **Elara Thorne**, with deep Council ties, saw the data and realized the existential threat: explore or starve. **Valerius Sterling Sr.**, seeing only the massive bounties, recognized a golden opportunity for glory and wealth, suspecting deeper reasons but caring only for the payout.

### **The Breakthrough (24 Months Ago)**

* **The Discovery:** A Vane scout ship detected the heat signature of the **Ash-Blood Isles**.  
* **The Hardship:** Integration was nearly impossible due to the distance and the Aether Beasts in the water.  
* **The Success:** When the Ash-Bloods accepted the "Cooling Suits" (Outward Flow) and Harmony burned their Obsidian (Inward Flow), the **Resonance** kicked in.  
* **The Safe Lane:** A literal corridor of calm water opened through the Aether storm, connecting Harmony Prime to the Ash-Blood Isles.

### **Current State: The Relocation & The Shattered Circuit**

* **The Great Move:** Using this new Safe Lane, **Vumbua Academy** (the mobile city) detached from the mainland and traveled to the Ash-Blood Isles.  
* **The Hope:** Vumbua is safe for the moment. The excitement is back up\! If they can keep the momentum going, the fear of the looming horizon will be a memory.  
* **The Dean's Secret (The Shattered Circuit):** Dean Isolde Vane has confirmed a terrifying mathematical reality. While the Ash-Blood and Mizizi Nodes are "Major" in size, they are outputting only **Minor Node power**.  
  * **The Leak:** Because these nodes were once part of a unified Empire, they are metaphysically "reaching out" to their missing siblings (Trench, Cloud, etc.). Energy is bleeding into the void, trying to bridge a gap that is too wide.  
  * **The Life Support:** The Nodes should have gone fully dark millennia ago. The only reason they are still functionally alive is the **Exchange Ritual**. The tenuous stories and the physical transfer of people kept a thin "Memory Thread" alive, keeping the Nodes on life support rather than letting them fully wither ("The Dark Ages").  
  * **The Ticking Clock:** Integrating a single clan (like the Ash-bloods) doesn't fix the leak; it only patches it. Each individual clan integration buys Harmony **1-2 years** of power at most. It is a stop-gap, not a solution.  
  * **The "Great Surge" Theory:** The only way to restore full output is to integrate **ALL SIX** of the Shattered Clans (**Mizizi**\-Root, **Pyre**\-Fire, **Trench**\-Earth, **Wadi**\-Water, **Renali**\-Air, and **Fulgar**\-Storm). Only when the full circuit is closed will the Nodes stop bleeding and come nearly fully back online.  
    * *The Promise:* Completing the set will trigger a surge of power not seen for thousands of years, ushering in a **500-Year Golden Age**.  
    * *The Cost:* Even this is temporary. The "Dark Ages" fossil record proves that entropy is inevitable. Once the 500 years end, the decline will begin again. Harmony‚Äôs choice will then be absolute: Double down on infinite exploration (Momentum) or accept that magic is a finite resource that eventually ends (Fate).  
* **The Player Hook:** In the **Great Library**, players can find a report titled *"The Bleached Atoll."* It details a small island found 50 years ago that had completely stagnated. The report notes that when Harmony tried to integrate it, the island simply crumbled into dust. It was too far gone. This is the fate Dean Vane fears for the Mizizi and Ash-bloods if they don't act fast.

# Daggerheart Communities

# **Communities**

### **Highborne**

Being part of a highborne community means you‚Äôre accustomed to a life of elegance, opulence, and prestige within the upper echelons of society. Traditionally, members of a highborne community possess incredible material wealth. While this can take a variety of forms depending on the community‚Äîincluding gold and other minerals, land, or controlling the means of production‚Äîthis status always comes with power and influence. Highborne place great value on titles and possessions, and there is little social mobility within their ranks. Members of a highborne community often control the political and economic status of the areas in which they live due to their ability to influence people and the economy with their substantial wealth. The health and safety of less affluent people who live in those locations often hinges on the ability of this highborne ruling class to prioritize the well-being of their subjects over profit.

Highborne are often amiable, candid, conniving, enterprising, ostentatious, and unflappable.

### **Community feature**

Privilege: You have advantage on rolls to consort with nobles, negotiate prices, or leverage your reputation to get what you want.

### 

### **Loreborne**

Being part of a loreborne community means you‚Äôre from a society that favors strong academic or political prowess. Loreborne communities highly value knowledge, frequently in the form of historical preservation, political advancement, scientific study, skill development, or lore and mythology compilation. Most members of these communities research in institutions built in bastions of civilization, while some eclectic few thrive in gathering information from the natural world. Some may be isolationists, operating in smaller enclaves, schools, or guilds and following their own unique ethos. Others still wield their knowledge on a larger scale, making deft political maneuvers across governmental landscapes.

Loreborne are often direct, eloquent, inquisitive, patient, rhapsodic, and witty.

### **Community feature**

Well-Read: You have advantage on rolls that involve the history, culture, or politics of a prominent person or place.

### **Orderborne**

Being part of an orderborne community means you‚Äôre from a collective that focuses on discipline or faith, and you uphold a set of principles that reflect your experience there. Orderborne are frequently some of the most powerful among the surrounding communities. By aligning the members of their society around a common value or goal, such as a god, doctrine, ethos, or even a shared business or trade, the ruling bodies of these enclaves can mobilize larger populations with less effort. While orderborne communities take a variety of forms‚Äîsome even profoundly pacifistic‚Äîperhaps the most feared are those that structure themselves around military prowess. In such a case, it‚Äôs not uncommon for orderborne to provide soldiers for hire to other cities or countries.

Orderborne are often ambitious, benevolent, pensive, prudent, sardonic, and stoic.

### **Community feature**

Dedicated: Record three sayings or values your upbringing instilled in you. Once per rest, when you describe how you‚Äôre embodying one of these principles through your current action, you can roll a \*\*d20\*\* as your Hope Die.

### **Ridgeborne**

Being part of a ridgeborne community means you‚Äôve called the rocky peaks and sharp cliffs of the mountainside home. Those who‚Äôve lived in the mountains often consider themselves hardier than most because they‚Äôve thrived among the most dangerous terrain many continents have to offer. These groups are adept at adaptation, developing unique technologies and equipment to move both people and products across difficult terrain. As such, ridgeborne grow up scrambling and climbing, making them sturdy and strong-willed. Ridgeborne localities appear in a variety of forms‚Äîsome cities carve out entire cliff faces, others construct castles of stone, and still more live in small homes on windblown peaks. Outside forces often struggle to attack ridgeborne groups, as the small militias and large military forces of the mountains are adept at utilizing their high-ground advantage.

Ridgeborne are often bold, hardy, indomitable, loyal, reserved, and stubborn.

### **Community feature**

Steady: You have advantage on rolls to traverse dangerous cliffs and ledges, navigate harsh environments, and use your survival knowledge.

### **Seaborne**

Being part of a seaborne community means you lived on or near a large body of water. Seaborne communities are built, both physically and culturally, around the specific waters they call home. Some of these groups live along the shore, constructing ports for locals and travelers alike. These harbors function as centers of commerce, tourist attractions, or even just a safe place to lay down one‚Äôs head after weeks of travel. Other seaborne live on the water in small boats or large ships, with the idea of ‚Äúhome‚Äù comprising a ship and its crew, rather than any one landmass. No matter their exact location, seaborne communities are closely tied to the ocean tides and the creatures who inhabit them. Seaborne learn to fish at a young age, and train from birth to hold their breath and swim in even the most tumultuous waters. Individuals from these groups are highly sought after for their sailing skills, and many become captains of vessels, whether within their own community, working for another, or even at the helm of a powerful naval operation.

Seaborne are often candid, cooperative, exuberant, fierce, resolute, and weathered.

### **Community feature**

Know the Tide: You can sense the ebb and flow of life. When you roll with Fear, place a token on your community card. You can hold a number of tokens equal to your level. Before you make an action roll, you can spend any number of these tokens to gain a \+1 bonus to the roll for each token spent. At the end of each session, clear all unspent tokens.

### **Slyborne**

Being part of a slyborne community means you come from a group that operates outside the law, including all manner of criminals, grifters, and con artists. Members of slyborne communities are brought together by their disparate goals and their clever means of achieving them. Many people in these communities have an array of unscrupulous skills: forging, thievery, smuggling, and violence. People of any social class can be slyborne, from those who have garnered vast wealth and influence to those without a coin to their name. To the outside eye, slyborne might appear to be ruffians with no loyalty, but these communities possess some of the strictest codes of honor which, when broken, can result in a terrifying end for the transgressor.

Slyborne are often calculating, clever, formidable, perceptive, shrewd, and tenacious.

### **Community feature**

Scoundrel: You have advantage on rolls to negotiate with criminals, detect lies, or find a safe place to hide.

### **Underborne**

Being part of an underborne community means you‚Äôre from a subterranean society. Many underborne live right beneath the cities and villages of other collectives, while some live much deeper. These communities range in size from small groups in burrows to massive metropolises in caverns of stone. In many locales, underborne are recognized for their incredible boldness and skill that enable great feats of architecture and engineering. Underborne are regularly hired for their bravery, as even the least daring among them has likely encountered formidable belowground beasts, and learning to dispatch such creatures is common practice amongst these societies. Because of the dangers of their environment, many underborne communities develop unique nonverbal languages that prove equally useful on the surface.

Underborne are often composed, elusive, indomitable, innovative, resourceful, and unpretentious.

### **Community feature**

Low-Light Living: When you‚Äôre in an area with low light or heavy shadow, you have advantage on rolls to hide, investigate, or perceive details within that area.

### **Wanderborne**

Being part of a wanderborne community means you‚Äôve lived as a nomad, forgoing a permanent home and experiencing a wide variety of cultures. Unlike many communities that are defined by their locale, wanderborne are defined by their traveling lifestyle. Because of their frequent migration, wanderborne put less value on the accumulation of material possessions in favor of acquiring information, skills, and connections. While some wanderborne are allied by a common ethos, such as a religion or a set of political or economic values, others come together after shared tragedy, such as the loss of their home or land. No matter the reason, the dangers posed by life on the road and the choice to continue down that road together mean that wanderborne are known for their unwavering loyalty.

Wanderborne are often inscrutable, magnanimous, mirthful, reliable, savvy, and unorthodox.

### **Community feature**

Nomadic Pack: Add a Nomadic Pack to your inventory. Once per session, you can spend a Hope to reach into this pack and pull out a mundane item that‚Äôs useful to your situation. Work with the GM to figure out what item you take out.

### **Wildborne**

Being part of a wildborne community means you lived deep within the forest. Wildborne communities are defined by their dedication to the conservation of their homelands, and many have strong religious or cultural ties to the fauna they live among. This results in unique architectural and technological advancements that favor sustainability over short-term, high-yield results. It is a hallmark of wildborne societies to integrate their villages and cities with the natural environment and avoid disturbing the lives of the plants and animals. While some construct their lodgings high in the branches of trees, others establish their homes on the ground beneath the forest canopy. It‚Äôs not uncommon for wildborne to remain reclusive and hidden within their woodland homes.

Wildborne are often hardy, loyal, nurturing, reclusive, sagacious, and vibrant.

### **Community feature**

Lightfoot: Your movement is naturally silent. You have advantage on rolls to move without being heard.

# Daggerheart Domain

### **Arcana**

Arcana is the domain of innate and instinctual magic. Those who choose this path tap into the raw, enigmatic forces of the realms to manipulate both their own energy and the elements. Arcana offers wielders a volatile power, but it is incredibly potent when correctly channeled. The Arcana domain can be accessed by the Druid and Sorcerer classes.

### **Blade**

Blade is the domain of weapon mastery. Whether by steel, bow, or perhaps a more specialized arm, those who follow this path have the skill to cut short the lives of others. Wielders of Blade dedicate themselves to achieving inexorable power over death. The Blade domain can be accessed by the Guardian and Warrior classes.

### **Bone**

Bone is the domain of tactics and the body. Practitioners of this domain have an uncanny control over their own physical abilities and an eye for predicting the behaviors of others in combat. Adherents to Bone gain an unparalleled understanding of bodies and their movements. The Bone domain can be accessed by the Ranger & Warrior classes.

### **Codex**

Codex is the domain of intensive magical study. Those who seek magical knowledge turn to the equations of power recorded in books, written on scrolls, etched into walls, or tattooed on bodies. Codex offers a commanding and versatile understanding of magic to devotees who pursue knowledge beyond the boundaries of common wisdom. The Codex domain can be accessed by the Bard and Wizard classes.

### **Grace**

Grace is the domain of charisma. Through rapturous storytelling, charming spells, or a shroud of lies, those who channel this power define the realities of their adversaries, bending perception to their will. Grace offers its wielders raw magnetism and mastery over language. The Grace domain can be accessed by the Bard and Rogue classes.

### **Midnight**

Midnight is the domain of shadows and secrecy. Whether by clever tricks, deft magic, or the cloak of night, those who channel these forces practice the art of obscurity and can uncover sequestered treasures. Midnight offers practitioners the power to control and create enigmas. The Midnight domain can be accessed by the Rogue and Sorcerer classes.

### **Sage**

Sage is the domain of the natural world. Those who walk this path tap into the unfettered power of the earth and its creatures to unleash raw magic. Sage grants its adherents the vitality of a blooming flower and the ferocity of a ravenous predator. The Sage domain can be accessed by the Druid and Ranger classes.

### **Splendor**

Splendor is the domain of life. Through this magic, followers gain the ability to heal and, to an extent, control death. Splendor offers its disciples the magnificent ability to both give and end life. The Splendor domain can be accessed by the Seraph and Wizard classes.

### **Valor**

Valor is the domain of protection. Whether through attack or defense, those who choose this discipline channel formidable strength to protect their allies in battle. Valor offers great power to those who raise their shields in defense of others. The Valor domain can be accessed by the Guardian and Seraph classes.

You can tell if a Captain runs Vanguard (engine hot and dirty, reckless) or Second Wave (perfect F-sharp hum, methodical). The Academy's main boiler is at 110%‚Äîa ticking bomb.*

   * 

   

7. WHY VUMBUA?  
     
   * **The Loyal Mechanic** *"Stabilization is Duty." My family keeps the engine running. I am here to learn frontier maintenance‚Äîbecause someone needs to fix what the explorers break.*  
   * *The Iron-Union philosophy is "Stabilization is Duty"‚Äîkeep the engine running, don't ask questions. But the boiler is at 110%. What do YOU believe will save the machine?*  
   *
