**Result:** Professor Ink (The Lantern) (3)

1. THE VUMBUA ACADEMY  
     
   * **Redirect**

   

2. THE VUMBUA ACADEMY  
     
   * **Begin Intake**

   

3. IDENTIFICATION REQUIRED  
     
   * **The Old World (Remnant Clans)** *Wild elemental forces. Ancient pacts. The world beyond the walls still remembers how to survive.*  
   * *The Academy recognizes two sources of cadet enrollment: those born within the Harmony Empire‚Äîthe refined civilization of industry and order‚Äîand those claimed from the Remnant Clans‚Äîthe wild lands where raw elemental forces hold sway.*  
   * 

   

4. CLAN LINEAGE SELECTION  
     
   * **The Mycelium Circle (Fungi)** *Tenders of the cycle of rot and rebirth. Your forest stopped decaying‚Äîa cancer of eternal growth that must be cut.*  
   * *Beyond the walls of Harmony, the old clans survive by bonding with raw elemental forces. Each biome shapes its people‚Äîand each clan carries a secret crisis that drove them to seek the Academy.*  
   * 

   

5. Identity Confirmed: THE MIZIZI  
     
   * **The Alchemist** *Learn Harmony's chemistry. Weaponize the corruption against itself‚Äîpoisons and cures are the same root.*  
   * *What You Know (The Spore-Mother):*  
   * *You live inside hollowed fossilized roots of ancient mega-flora, using fungal spores for communication and defense. You are the recyclers of the world‚Äîmedicine, food, the cycle of decay and regrowth. Your people use specialized, nature-based efficiency: bioluminescence instead of lightbulbs, beast-labor instead of engines. But without decay, there is no new life.*  
   * *Family Dogma (What you were taught):*  
   * *"All life is a cycle. We tend the forest, and the forest tends us and keeps us away from the world that wants to stop the cycle of rebirth and decay."*  
   * *Hidden Reality (What you suspect):*  
   * *The Petrified Forest has stopped decaying‚Äîit's a cancer of eternal growth. Shortly after, Harmony's "Iron-Beasts" (iron walkers) breached the forest edges; your elders made a deal to buy Harmony herbicides because natural magic can't bring about the cycle of death that you believe is the key to life.*

   

6. LOGISTICS: HOW DID YOU ARRIVE?  
     
   * **The Root Network** *The old ways. You entered the Spore-Mother's network and emerged three hundred miles away in the Academy's compost pit. You still taste the mycelium.*  
   * *The Petrified Forest is a cancer of eternal growth‚Äîit has stopped decaying, and without decay there is no new life. Your Circle emerged from the trees to agree to the Paperman's contract because you lack the fire and chemicals to prune the corruption yourselves. you expect he Academy will be terrifyingly sterile.*  
   * 

   

7. WHY VUMBUA?  
     
   * **The Infiltrator** *I carry the Spore-Mother within me. Harmony thinks I came to learn. But I am a seed‚Äîand this sterile Academy will bloom whether it wants to or not.*  
   * *The White Scorch taboo says never trust Fire-Kin‚Äîthey bring eternal life. But the Petrified Forest needs burning. Your Circle joined Harmony because you lack the flame. What do YOU believe will save the cycle?*  
   * 

   

8. PROFICIENCY ASSESSMENT (MIZIZI)  
     
   * **Toxicology** *Poisons and cures.*

   

9. PROJECTION COMPLETE

    * **Golden \- Druid**  
    * **Silver \- Druid**

# Ignatious

Based on the setting notes and the session 0 transcript, here is the lore breakdown for the Ash Bloods (Volcano Clan), separated by what is commonly known/believed by the PC (Ignatius) and what secrets or deeper lore are currently hidden or serve as subtext.

### **The Ash Bloods (Volcano Clan / The Pyre-Keepers)**

**PC Representative:** Ignatius (played by John Hagey) **Ancestry:** Emberkin (Half-obsidian appearance) **Biome:** Volcanic Isles (off the main continent) **Node:** Heat/Fire

---

#### **1\. Known History & Beliefs (What Ignatius Knows)**

* **The Age of Embers:** According to clan lore, there was once a time of "great heat and flame." However, when the clan stopped communicating with others and went into isolation, the flames went "cold" and turned to embers. For generations, heating a simple pot of water required massive boulders of heat-rock.  
* **The Arrival of Harmony:** When Harmony‚Äôs ships arrived, the volcanoes physically reacted. The embers became hot again. The clan attributes this reinvigoration directly to the arrival of outsiders, validating their lore that isolation causes the cold.  
* **Current Relationship:** Of all the clans, the Ash Bloods are the most excited about Harmony. They have an active "normal trade" relationship, exchanging their hyper-specialized heat rocks and labor for Harmony‚Äôs "generalized energy" (batteries/petrol) and medicine,.  
* **The "Contract of Blood":** The clan maintains strict bloodline exchanges (marriage/partners) with outsiders to prevent corruption and inbreeding, viewing social presence as vital to their survival.

#### **2\. The Internal Conflict (The Softening)**

* **Reliance on Tech:** Harmony technology has made life significantly easier. A "pebble" of heat now does the work of a boulder.  
* **Cultural Anxiety:** While the clan is physically thriving due to better medicine and food, the Elders fear the youth are becoming "soft." The effort required to maintain the embers defined their character; now that the fires burn effortlessly with Harmony tech, that discipline is fading.

#### **3\. Ignatius‚Äôs Specific Perspective (PC Motivation)**

* **The Rebel Theory:** Unlike the rest of his clan, Ignatius believes the "reinvigoration" of the volcano is a lie. He believes Harmony‚Äôs fuel source is "fake" and that the clan is swapping out their sacred, real fuel for an artificial substitute.  
* **The Pilgrimage:** Ignatius got into trouble for exploring forbidden areas to prove this theory. He frames his banishment to the Academy not as punishment, but as a "pilgrimage" to find a *new, true* source of heat to return the clan to the "way it should be",.

---

#### **4\. Hidden Lore & Subtext (For Later Reveal)**

* **The "Curse of Ash":** The clan deeply fears that if the world stops expanding, the "Curse of Ash" will return, freezing their vents entirely. This ties directly to the Harmony "Minimum" crisis‚Äîif the civilization stops expanding/stitching the world together, the power fails.  
* **The Nature of the Node:** The clan believes the fire is a living entity that requires "social presence" to survive. This may explain why the volcano flared when Harmony arrived‚Äînot because of Harmony's *tech*, but because of the connection/stitching to the wider world.  
* **Fate of Previous Students:** The Ash Bloods have sent students to Vumbua Academy before. It is noted that "so far no one's come back, not really," though they send letters. Whether they have simply fully integrated into Harmony society or something more nefarious has happened to them remains ambiguous.  
* **Economic Reality:** While Harmony uses the Ash Bloods' labor, the Ash Bloods technically hold an "infinite resource" (magma/heat), whereas Harmony‚Äôs batteries are merely more efficient storage that is currently "running lean",. The balance of power may shift if Harmony hits "The Minimum."

# Aggie and Britt

Based on the session 0 transcript and setting notes, here is the lore breakdown for the Mizizi (Deep-Root/Mycelium Clan), distinguishing between the PCs' known reality and the hidden subtext.

### **The Mizizi (The Deep-Root Clan / The Mycelium)**

**PC Representatives:** **Aggie** (played by Kristina/Luke S audio source) and **Britt** (played by Sophie Foreman Noone). **Ancestry:** Described as "Turtle-Mushroom Folk" (Mechanically likely a Galapa/Fungril mix). They reside in fossilized mega-flora and hollowed-out roots. **Biome:** The Petrifaction Fields / Fungal Deep. **Node:** Earth/Growth (Corrupted or Wild).

---

#### **1\. The Characters: Aggie & Britt**

* **Visual Distinction:**  
  * **Aggie (Kristina):** Looks more like a red-and-white spotted mushroom (resembling a Mario mushroom) combined with a turtle. She is physically quieter, tending to "waddle" toward dark, safe corners when overwhelmed.  
  * **Britt (Sophie):** Similar fungal-turtle physiology but colored gray, dusty, and powdery. She is more outwardly aggressive and cynical.  
* **Relationship:** They are cousins who grew up together (referenced as attending "turtle camp"). They were not previously "best friends" but were forced together by age and circumstance. However, they have bonded over a shared secret suspicion of Harmony.  
* **Motivations:**  
  * **Britt:** Believes "the call is coming from inside the house." She views her attendance at the Academy as an infiltration mission to uncover the conspiracy behind Harmony.  
  * **Aggie:** Shares this skepticism but is quieter about it. She believes Harmony is responsible for the imbalance in their world and wants to find out how.

#### **2\. Known History & Beliefs (What Aggie & Britt Know)**

* **The Philosophy of Decay:** The clan holds a fervent belief that "things must die." Their lore states, "when things stop dying, we start dying." They view their survival as dependent on the natural cycle of death and decay.  
* **The Forest‚Äôs Failure:** For centuries, the fossilized forest kept them segregated from the world. Recently, the forest "failed" to keep outsiders out, which the clan interprets as the world stopping its natural death cycle.  
* **The Trade Deal:** Harmony explorers (led by a "Paper Man" in a sterile suit) established contact. The clan entered a trade agreement: Harmony takes soil, roots, bark, and stone. In exchange, Harmony provides weapons and tools to help the clan destroy/prune their own home. The PCs view themselves as a "fire brigade," trying to kill the forest growth that has become unmanageable.  
* **The Academy Invitation:** This is not the first time the Mizizi have sent students to Vumbua, but previous students haven't returned (though they send letters). Aggie and Britt were elected to join this year's massive intake.

#### **3\. Hidden Lore & Subtext (For Later Reveal)**

* **The Nature of the Node:** The SRD notes their Node is "Earth/Growth (Corrupted or Wild)". This explains why the forest is overgrowing and requires constant culling. The "failure" of the forest to keep people out is actually the Node becoming active or corrupted, possibly reacting to Harmony's proximity.  
* **The "Paper Man":** The initial contact was made by a man described as "sterile," wearing metal (which the clan does not use). This creates a thematic conflict between the *preservation/sterility* of Harmony (who fear the "Minimum" and loss of power) and the *decay/cycle* philosophy of the Mizizi.  
* **The "Recyclers":** The Mizizi are described in the setting notes as the "recyclers" of the world. Harmony‚Äôs crisis is "Stagnation" (expansion stops, reality dissolves). The Mizizi belief that "things must die" is the direct antithesis to Harmony's fear of the "Ether/Nether" dissolution. Harmony tries to stitch the world together to stop it from fading; the Mizizi believe things *must* fade to allow for life.  
* **The Unstoppable Growth:** Outside the forest, Harmony industry is trying to harvest wood, but the forest grows back faster than they can cut it. This suggests the Node is currently over-active or defensive, contradicting Harmony's belief that new Nodes are "shattered" or "weak".

# Iggy

Based on the session 0 transcript and the setting notes, here is the lore breakdown for **Holly Strebel‚Äôs character** (referred to here as the "Deepkin" or Earthkin) and **Ignatius** (John Hagey‚Äôs character), separating their known reality from the hidden subtext.

### **The "Deepkin" / Earthkin (The Subterranean/Mud Clan)**

**PC Representative:** Holly Strebel‚Äôs Character (Unnamed in transcript, described as "The Mole" archetype). **Ancestry:** Earthkin (described as semi-human shaped but made of packed dirt/mud that is constantly crumbling). **Biome:** Deep Underground / Underwater (Requires pressurized goggles and moisture to survive on the surface). **Node:** Water/Earth (Linked to the River Clan via treaty).

---

#### **1\. Character Details: "The Mole"**

* **Physiology:** He is chronically sickly and physically overwhelmed by the surface environment. He possesses giant bug eyes that require pressurized fluid injections (via goggles) and skin that steams in the sun, requiring constant application of a mud-like sunscreen.  
* **Personality:** Grumpy, comedic, and secretive. He constantly mumbles to himself and curses the environment. He is paranoid, taking zigzagging routes to cover his tracks.  
* **Arrival:** He emerged from the water at a dock. An old man (possibly a plant or just a bystander) threw a heavy trench coat over him, which provided him a moment of physical contentment due to the weight/pressure.

#### **2\. Known History & Beliefs (What He Knows)**

* **Isolation:** His clan has almost zero contact with the surface world. He is completely alien to Harmony society.  
* **The Bridal Exchange:** The only contact his people have with others is a "blood exchange" bridal ceremony with the **River Clan** (The Wadi). Once a year, someone jumps into the water, and his clan pulls them down, while one of his people goes to the shore, never to return. This acts as a genetic exchange to prevent population collapse.  
* **Motivation:** He wants to absorb as much information as possible about the surface world, though his specific mission is secretive. He is effectively "going rogue" or acting on motives potentially unapproved by his clan.

#### **3\. Hidden Lore & Subtext (For Later Reveal)**

* **The "Lost Bond":** The setting notes mention the River Clan (Wadi) lost their bond with the Air Clan, causing their river to dry up into the "Dry Vein". Holly‚Äôs character likely represents the *other* half of the River Clan's survival strategy‚Äîthe deep underground water sources.  
* **The "Old Man":** The man at the dock who gave him the coat was unbothered by a mud-creature emerging from the sea. This suggests either that Harmony has better surveillance than the PC thinks, or that there are sympathizers watching for the "Deepkin."  
* **The Node Status:** The River Clan‚Äôs Node is described as "Weak/Trickling". Holly‚Äôs character may be the key to why the water retreated underground, or he may unknowingly carry the connection to a deeper, more stable Water Node.

---

### **The Ash Bloods (The Volcano Clan)**

**PC Representative:** **Ignatius** (played by John Hagey). **Ancestry:** Emberkin (Half-obsidian appearance). **Biome:** Volcanic Isles (off the main continent). **Node:** Heat/Fire.

---

#### **1\. Character Details: Ignatius ("Iggy")**

* **Personality:** A rebellious teenager. He views himself as a "new kid on the block" who is in awe of the city but fiercely critical of its artificiality.  
* **Motivation:** He believes he is on a "pilgrimage." While the Elders banished him for exploring forbidden areas and "fleeing," he reframes this as a holy mission to find a *true* source of heat to replace the "fake" Harmony fuel.

#### **2\. Known History & Beliefs (What Ignatius Knows)**

* **The Age of Embers:** Ignatius knows the clan‚Äôs fires were merely embers until Harmony arrived. Harmony‚Äôs technology "reinvigorated" the volcano, making life easier.  
* **The "Fake" Flame:** Unlike his clan, who embraced Harmony with excitement and trade, Ignatius believes Harmony‚Äôs "Crystal Batteries" (which act like little suns) are a false religion. He believes the clan is trading their cultural soul for easy heating.  
* **Trade Relations:** The Ash Bloods provide labor and hyper-specialized heat rocks. In exchange, they get Harmony‚Äôs "generalized energy" (batteries/petrol) which is currently more efficient than their rocks.

#### **3\. Hidden Lore & Subtext (For Later Reveal)**

* **The "Curse of Ash":** The Elders‚Äô obsession with Harmony isn't just about comfort; it is fear. They believe if the world stops expanding (Stagnation), the "Curse of Ash" will return, freezing their vents entirely.  
* **Social Fire:** The clan believes the Node is a living entity that requires "social presence" to survive. The volcano didn't flare because of Harmony's *tech*, but because of the connection to the wider world. Ignatius‚Äôs isolationist views might actually threaten the Node if he isn't careful.  
* **Infinite Resource vs. The Minimum:** Harmony is facing "The Minimum" (energy crisis). Ignatius believes his clan is the weaker partner, but in reality, the Ash Bloods possess an "infinite resource" (magma), while Harmony‚Äôs batteries are running lean. Ignatius is unknowingly sitting on the solution to Harmony's impending collapse.

# Loami

Based on the session 0 transcript and the setting notes, here is the lore breakdown for **Lomi** (played by Luke Foreman) and his "clan" (The Harmony/City Working Class).

### **The Harmony (The City of Vumbua / The Infrastructure)**

**PC Representative:** **Lomi** (spelled L-O-M-I in the transcript). **Ancestry:** **Earthkin** (or Earthkin/Human mix). **Biome:** The City of Harmony (specifically the Boiler Room/Underground). **Node:** Crystal Batteries (The Central Network).

---

#### **1\. Character Details: Lomi**

* **Visuals:** Lomi is described as a "blue-collar grease monkey" who appears perpetually dirty. The distinction between his skin and the dirt is blurred, described as being in a "perpetual state of messiness".  
* **Background:** He is older than the average student (described as the "25-year-old at boot camp"). He comes from a long line of boiler workers; his family home hangs schematics of the original boilers on the wall rather than art.  
* **Personality:** He is "Union Strong" and pragmatic. He scolds people for littering or disrespecting public infrastructure, reminding them that the city wouldn't run without people like him.  
* **Motivation:** He views himself as the "big smart guy" regarding mechanics. His family encouraged him to join the Academy because "someone's got to fix the ship if it goes wrong." He is there to ensure the infrastructure of exploration survives.

#### **2\. Known History & Beliefs (What Lomi Knows)**

* **The History of Harmony:** Unlike the isolated clans, Lomi knows Harmony has a history spanning thousands of years. He knows the civilization functions like "cities that eat other cities" in terms of energy‚Äîthe culture revolves entirely around finding and assimilating new lands.  
* **The Contracting World:** Lomi is aware of a phenomenon where islands and landmasses physically get closer to the Harmony Core over time. What used to be distant islands are now much closer in mileage. He knows this is a fact of their world, even if the metaphysical "why" is debated.  
* **The "New Buzz":** He joined the Academy now because he sensed a shift. After 80 years of stagnation where no new civilizations were found, there is a sudden "reinvigorated buzz" about exploration, and he wants to be part of the solution.

#### **3\. Hidden Lore & Subtext (For Later Reveal)**

* **The "Minimum" Crisis:** Lomi works in the boiler room, meaning he is physically closest to Harmony's deepest secret: the power is failing. While he may attribute flickering lights or engine stalls to mechanical maintenance issues, the reality is that Harmony is hitting "The Minimum." The civilization has stopped expanding, so the "batteries" are running out of metaphysical charge.  
* **The Nature of the "Stitching":** Lomi knows the world gets closer together, but the hidden lore is that this is the "Great Stitching." New Nodes act as gravity wells for reality. If Harmony stops exploring, the "stitching" fails, and reality will begin to dissolve into the "Ether/Nether".  
* **The Academy's Desperation:** Lomi likely believes he got in because of his skill. The hidden reality is that the Academy has radically shifted its admissions policy to a "Great Cull" strategy. They are desperate for bodies to throw at the frontier because early scans of the new territory suggest the Nodes there are "shattered" or weak. They aren't looking for "Glory Seekers" anymore; they need "Survivalists" like Lomi to keep the lights on.

# **The Loom's Registry: Class of '52**

**Total Enrollment:** 102,419 Candidates **Academy Goal:** Resource Extraction & Reality Stabilization **Current Crisis:** "The Minimum" (Power Failure Imminent)

## **üèõÔ∏è I. Faculty & Administration**

* **Mannerism:** Grips the podium until her knuckles turn white; never looks a student directly in the eye for more than a second.  
* **Backstory:** A former Exploranaut who "retired" after a disastrous mission. She is obsessed with metrics to hide the fact that Vumbua is dying.  
* **Flaw:** Perfectionism. Will sacrifice a squad to maintain a "clean" data report.

**3\. Celia Vance** (Compliance Proctor)

**3\. Bramble** (Druid/Silver)

* **Backstory:** A specialist in "Genetic Purity." He breeds plants that grow in perfect grids.

  ### **üî• Squad 06: "The Kiln" (Integrated Seraphs)**

* **Vibe:** "Safe" fire. Tame, compliant Ash-Bloods.  
* **Loom Defense:** "Controlled Burn Unit. 'Wild' thermal signatures suppressed."

**1\. Cinder-4 (Leader)** (Seraph/Silver)

* **Backstory:** An Ash-Blood who abandoned his clan‚Äôs name for a number. He believes civilization is the only way to survive the "fading heat" of the world.

**2\. Hearth** (Seraph/Silver)

* **Backstory:** Seeking the comfort of the "Steady Flame." She hates the volatile, explosive nature of her ancestors.

**3\. Kindle** (Seraph/Silver)

* **Backstory:** A young student who is mesmerized by the "Clean Light" of Harmony tech, viewing her own clan's fire as dirty.

  ### **üåä Squad 07: "The Bathysphere" (Pressure Specialists)**

* **Vibe:** Grit, salt, and heavy machinery. They love the high-pressure "Minimum."  
* **Loom Defense:** "Sub-aquatic retrieval. Pressure-tolerant physiology."

**1\. Captain Barnacle (Leader)** (Warrior/Silver)

* **Backstory:** A Trench-Kin veteran. He is only here because the deep trenches are running out of air, and he needs Harmony's pumps.

**2\. Pressure** (Warrior/Silver)

* **Backstory:** A competitive spirit who wants to show that the "Deep Folk" are physically superior to the "Surface Softies."

**3\. Depth** (Warrior/Silver)

* **Backstory:** A dreamer who believes the "Great Stitching" is actually pulling things toward a sunken paradise.

  ### **üí∞ Squad 08: "The Legacy" (The Nepo-Babies)**

* **Vibe:** High-end gear, low-end skill. Nepo-babies and party-goers.  
* **Loom Defense:** "Political Appeasement Protocol. Enrollment guarantees funding."

**1\. Percival Vane-Smythe III (Leader)** (Bard/Gold \- Purchased)

* **Backstory:** Exploring is "trendy" this season. He wants the outfit and the stories, but none of the actual dirt.

**2\. Lady Glimmer** (Wizard/Silver)

* **Backstory:** She is here to "Network." She views the Ether as a backdrop for the most exclusive party of the century.

**3\. Baron Bolt** (Guardian/Silver)

* **Backstory:** The only one with a heart. He was hired/guilt-tripped into shielding his "friends" from their own incompetence.

  ### **üõ°Ô∏è Squad 09: "The Ablative" (The Grunts)**

* **Vibe:** Nervous, sweating, and clutching second-hand weapons. The "Expendables."  
* **Loom Defense:** "Trap Detection via Mass. Deploying low-value assets first."

**1\. "Sarge" (Leader)** (Warrior/Rust)

* **Voice:** Weary "Old Soldier" rasp. *"Down here, we‚Äôre all just leak-in' grease."*  
* **Backstory:** Former Silver-rank scout demoted to Rust as a scapegoat.  
* **Bond:** His squad. **Flaw:** Fatalism. **Motive:** Retire.

**2\. Lucky** (Ranger/Rust)

* **Voice:** Cockney street urchin. *"Spare a bit o‚Äô gleam for a starv-in' scholar, in-nit?"*  
* **Backstory:** Street urchin who pickpocketed his way in.  
* **Bond:** Sister in Low-Bunks. **Flaw:** Grifter.

**3\. Pudge** (Warrior/Rust)

* **Voice:** Whiny and fast. *"Y-y-you gonna eat that?"*  
* **Backstory:** Son of a farmer. Hungry since age six.  
* **Bond:** Mother‚Äôs copper spoon. **Flaw:** Cowardice.

# Ahs Bloods

Based on the **Vumbua Academy** lore and **Session 0** notes, here is the breakdown of the Ash-Blood (Pyre-Keeper) presence at the Academy, their internal conflicts, and how they relate to **Ignatius**.

### **Overview: The Ash-Blood Diaspora**

The Ash-Bloods are currently the "celebrities" of the intake. Because their "Integration" (The Stitching) was a recent, massive success that physically reignited their volcanoes, they are generally viewed by Harmony as the model minority‚Äîproof that the Empire works.

However, a deep ideological schism exists between those who embrace Harmony (The Integrated) and those who fear it (The Heretics/Rebels).

---

### **1\. Key Ash-Blood NPCs**

#### **A. Lady Ignis (The Matriarch)**

* **Role:** Representative of the Clans on the High Council.  
* **Rank:** Political VIP (Above Academy Ranks).  
* **Relation to Ignatius:** She is the Matriarch. Ignatius would know her well; she likely signed off on his "pilgrimage" (banishment).  
* **Motive:** **Survival via Politics.** She enacted the "Expansion Bill" to move the Academy to the Ash-Blood Isles. She believes political power is the only way to ensure her people are partners, not fuel.  
* **Campaign Fit:** She represents the "Establishment." If Ignatius rebels against Harmony, he is directly embarrassing her and endangering the treaty she forged \[`842`\].

#### **B. Pyrrhus (The Heretic)**

* **Role:** Unregistered Scholar / Laborer. Found in the **Great Library**.  
* **Rank:** None (Likely hiding among the workforce or Copper tier).  
* **Relation to Ignatius:** A warning. Pyrrhus was an ex-priest banished for claiming the Ancestors were "screaming." Ignatius likely heard rumors of him as a cautionary tale of what happens when you resist.  
* **Motive:** **Expose the Parasite.** He believes the heat isn't fading naturally; it is being *diverted* to feed the Spire.  
* **Campaign Fit:** He is the primary hook for the "Energy Crisis" plot. He drops the map fragment showing the "Heat Sink" under the Dean‚Äôs office \[`1004`, `1033`\].

#### **C. Squad 06: "The Kiln" (The Rivals)**

* **Role:** The "Model Students." They are the foil to Ignatius. They wear full containment suits and refuse to use "wild fire."  
* **Class/Rank:** **Silver / Seraphs** \[`939`\].  
* **Members:**  
  1. **Cinder-4 (Leader):** Abandoned his clan name for a number to fit the Loom‚Äôs catalog. He believes civilization is the only shield against the cold.  
  2. **Hearth:** Seeks the comfort of a "Steady Flame" over volcanic bursts.  
  3. **Kindle:** Mesmerized by the "Clean Light" of Harmony tech; views clan fire as dirty.  
* **Interaction:** Cinder-4 confronts Ignatius in the locker rooms: *"Stop showing off that wild flame, brother. Put on the containment suit."* \[`945`\].

#### **D. Lady Glissade (The Captain)**

* **Role:** Explorer Captain (The "North Ice" bet).  
* **Status:** Integrated Ash-Blood.  
* **Motive:** **Temperature Regulation.** She uses her natural Ash-Blood heat to survive harvesting glacial ice without freezing, proving Ash-Bloods have utility beyond just boilers.  
* **Campaign Fit:** A potential mentor who uses her heritage for industry rather than combat \[`947`\].

---

### **2\. How Many Are There?**

While the exact number isn't listed, we can extrapolate from the demographics:

* **Total Intake:** 100,000 candidates.  
* **Ash-Blood Presence:** They are a minority, but a visible one.  
* **Squad 06 ("The Kiln"):** 3 Members.  
* **Ignatius:** 1 Member.  
* **Pyrrhus:** 1 Member.  
* **Background Students:** There is a "small circle" of Ash-Bloods mentioned at the bonfire trying to light a True Spark, distinct from the majority using Safe-Flame \[`1000`\].  
* **Estimated Count:** Likely **50‚Äì100** total candidates. They are rare enough to be "minor celebrities" but numerous enough to form a clique \[`969`, `1000`\].

### **3\. Who "Did Not Make The Cut"?**

Based on the Academy's attrition rates \[`931`, `987`\]:

* **The Rust Tier (20% Failure Rate):** About **20%** of the Ash-Blood candidates likely failed the "Spire Scan."  
* **Fate of the Failed:** They were not sent home. They were reassigned to **City Maintenance** (The Boiler Rooms).  
* **Why this matters to Ignatius:** The Boiler Room runs on **Direct Obsidian Transfer** \[`841`\]. The "failed" Ash-Bloods are actually the most critical workers in the city, physically feeding the engines with their heat. Ignatius will likely find many of his "failed" kin working alongside **Lomi** in the under-city, keeping the school alive while the "Gold" students get the glory.

### **4\. Ignatius‚Äôs Knowledge & Perspective**

* **How he knows them:** The clan is small enough that he would recognize Cinder-4 and Pyrrhus by sight or reputation. He knows Lady Ignis personally as the Matriarch.  
* **The Friction:** Ignatius is unique because he is a **Gold Rank** (Visionary) who holds **Heretical Views**.  
  * **Squad 06** sees him as dangerous‚Äîa "Wild Element" that could ruin their integration status.  
  * **Pyrrhus** sees him as a potential savior‚Äîsomeone with the rank/access to prove the Spire is stealing their heat.  
  * **Lady Ignis** sees him as a liability‚Äîa rebellious child who needs to grow up before he destroys the treaty.

# Captains

# ***‚öì The Captains' Manifest: The Proving Voyage***

***Phase:** The 1-Month "Proving Voyage" (Internship).*

***Objective:** Field testing in the "Safe Zone" and Periphery before the deep expedition.*

***The "Captain's Boon":** Each Captain has a discretionary pool of **50 Loom Points** to award to a single candidate (or split amongst a squad) who demonstrates exceptional promise. This Boon acts as a "Direct Commission."*

## ***üïµÔ∏è Key Captain Dossiers & Secret Agendas***

### ***1\. Valerius Sterling (The Glory Hound)***

* ***The Pitch:** "Join the elite. We have the best food, the best press, and the least chance of death."*  
* ***The Secret:** He isn't actually exploring. He's re-visiting a "Safe Node" discovered 20 years ago and pretending it's new for the cameras.*  
* ***The Risk:** Zero danger, but zero respect from real explorers.*

### ***2\. Kaelo "Ghost" Vane (The Spy)***

* ***The Pitch:** "The Academy needs eyes, not heroes. Help me see what the River Clan is hiding."*  
* ***The Secret:** Kaelo suspects the River Clan has a weapon that can ground the Sky-Spire.*  
* ***The Risk:** If caught, the Academy will disavow you. You will be left behind.*

### ***3\. Ignis "Scorch" (The Daredevil)***

* ***The Pitch:** "We are going to run the engine at 120% until it melts or we win."*  
* ***The Secret:** His engine is melting. He needs an Elemental (Ignatius) or a Mechanic (Loami) to physically hold it together during the climb.*  
* ***The Risk:** High probability of explosion. High probability of glory.*

### ***4\. Elara Thorne (The Saint)***

* ***The Pitch:** "We are bringing food and medicine to the 'Rust' populations stranded outside the gates."*  
* ***The Secret:** She is smuggling unregistered "Rust" candidates back into the city disguised as patients.*  
* ***The Risk:** You become an accomplice to treason against the Loom's sorting protocols.*

### ***5\. Professor Althea Ink (The Xenobotanist)***

* ***The Pitch:** "The Mizizi fear the 'Old Growth' because they say it whispers. I say it reads. Help me prove the forest is a library before the Verdant Trust mulches it."*  
* ***The Secret:** She is secretly working with **Rill** (the River-Born adoptee). Rill provides the coordinates; Ink provides the ship. They are trying to extract a "Core Sample" from an Ancient Tree to prove it contains data, not just wood.*  
* ***The Risk:** The "Whispers" in the Old Growth are psychic data-dumps. Low-Willpower characters might get overwritten by ancient history.*

### ***6\. "Old Man" Silas (The Scrapper)***

* ***The Pitch:** "I ain't got a speech. Get on the boat or don't."*  
* ***The Secret:** Silas has found a "Pre-Stitch" vault in the trash vortex. He needs a crew stupid enough to help him haul it out.*  
* ***The Risk:** Tetanus. Also, the vault might be booby-trapped.*

### ***7\. Captain "Iron-Lung" Jorah (The Submariner)***

* ***The Pitch:** "The surface is a lie. The heat is down deep. Join me in the dark."*  
* ***The Secret:** He is searching for the "Deep-Mother," a mythical creature the Trench-Kin worship.*  
* ***The Risk:** Structural implosion. Total darkness.*

### ***8\. Captain "Iron-Hide" (The Shield)***

* ***The Pitch:** "We don't run. We tank. I bring everyone home, even if I have to carry the ship myself."*  
* ***The Secret:** He isn't looking for a Node; he's field-testing a new "Ablative Hull" made of compressed Ash-blood obsidian.*  
* ***The Loami Hook:** Iron-Hide is a living legend among the Iron-Union. He started as a Copper-rank boiler scrubber (just like Loami). He famously saved the last expedition by manually holding a cracked thermal vent shut with his own geomantic skin for 6 hours. He also wrote "The Percussive Maintenance Guide (Vol. 4)," which is likely the only textbook Loami actually likes.*  
* ***The Risk:** You will take damage. A lot of it. But you won't die.*  
* ***Iggy Hook:** THIS is the boat that first disrupted the tides above the deepkin shelf. It returned regularly and it is how he hitch-hiked to shore (which was massively impressive to do considering the weaponry and defenses)*

## ***üé≤ The 50-Point Boon (Mechanic)***

*When the players choose a Captain, they must "Interview" (Roleplay \+ Roll).*

* ***Great Success (DC 18+):** The Captain grants the **Full Boon (+50 Points)** to the character.*  
  * *Effect: This guarantees Gold Rank for anyone (even Loami).*  
* ***Success (DC 12-17):** The Captain grants a **Partial Boon (+20 Points)**.*  
  * *Effect: Enough to bump a Silver to Gold or a Copper to Silver.*  
* ***Failure (DC \< 12):** The Captain accepts them as "Grunt Labor" (0 Points).*  
  * *Effect: They are just along for the ride. No rank increase.*

***Squad Dilemma:***

*Since **Squad 7-Alpha** must deploy together, they must convince a Captain to take all of them.*

* ***Valerius** won't take Loami (Copper).*  
* ***Ghost** thinks Britt is too loud.*  
* ***Ink** loves Iggy but fears Ignatius will burn his specimens.*  
* ***Silas** will take anyone, but offers no prestige.*

*This forces the players to leverage their connections to get the whole squad hired by a "Good" captain, or settle for the "Bad" one.*

# Living NPC latest

Based on the transcripts from **Session 0 (vumbua 1\)** and the provided lore, here is the complete list of NPCs your players have directly interacted with or observed closely, along with what was said and learned.

### **I. Key Narrative NPCs (Plot Critical)**

#### **1\. Dean Isolde Vane**

* **Role:** Head of the Academy.  
* **Interaction:** Gave the welcome speech in the Great Hall.  
* **What She Said:**  
  * "For 80 years our maps have been static."  
  * "We‚Äôve missed the thrill of adventure. I‚Äôve been lonely."  
  * "We don't know what the Mizizi do, and that's amazing."  
  * **The Threat:** "We have to lose another 20,000 of you by the end of the week."  
* **What Players Learned:** She acts bubbly and energetic (like a female Professor Heimerdinger), but Britt explicitly whispered, *"I don't trust this f\*\*\*ing guy."* She framed the intake as a desperate need for new discovery after a long drought \[`1170`, `1171`\].

#### **2\. Rill (The River-Born)**

* **Role:** Dean‚Äôs Attendant / Mizizi Clan Member.  
* **Interaction:** Appeared from behind the curtain to pull the Dean back. She waved to Britt and Aggie.  
* **What Players Learned:**  
  * **Transformation:** She looks much healthier and well-dressed (blue romper, turban) than when she left the forest 2 years ago as an outcast.  
  * **Status:** She has a very familiar, close relationship with the Dean (locking arms).  
  * **Recognition:** She knows Britt and Aggie personally and waved "good luck" to them \[`1173`, `1174`\].

#### **3\. Sarge (Squad 09 Leader)**

* **Role:** Warrior / Former Maintenance Worker.  
* **Interaction:** Met **Lomi** outside the exams. They know each other from workers' campfires.  
* **What He Said:**  
  * "Loaves? Loaves, we made it."  
  * Admitted he barely passed: "I don't even know what I was talking about. You always guess C, right?"  
  * "I gotta remember why I'm here. Doing this for the lads."  
* **What Players Learned:** He is insecure about his academic ability but driven by duty. He represents the "Common Man" trying to break into the elite ranks \[`1163`, `1164`\].

#### **4\. Lucky**

* **Role:** Street Urchin / Hustler.  
* **Interaction:** Approached **Iggy** and the group outside the Great Hall. Tried to sell Iggy a "Kleenex" (a stolen guard's turban).  
* **What He Said:**  
  * "I'm Lucky. You need something? You let Lucky know."  
  * "If you find something cool, I'm your guy."  
* **What Players Learned:** He is a scavenger and black-market dealer. He accepted Iggy's useless invention (the noise-making trumpet) in trade. He is fast and slippery \[`1180`, `1182`\].

#### **5\. Serra (Seraphina) Fox**

* **Role:** Student / "Ally."  
* **Interaction:** Approached the group at the crane. Invited them to the bonfire.  
* **What She Said:**  
  * "Oh my god. Are you... from the Island? And are you Ash Blood? Three of you all in one group? Oh, what a splendorous occasion\!"  
  * "I'm an ally. Is that okay to say?"  
* **What Players Learned:** She is fascinated by the Clans (almost fetishizing them). She is nervous but eager. **Ignatius** explicitly stated: *"I don't trust this b\*\*\*\*."* \[`1202`, `1206`\].

---

### **II. Atmospheric NPCs (Flavor & World Building)**

#### **6\. The "Chad" Student**

* **Role:** Aristocrat / Gold Tier vibe.  
* **Interaction:** Spoke to **Ignatius** in the courtyard.  
* **What He Said:**  
  * "Welcome to the show, mate."  
  * "Oh... will your hand burn me?" (After Ignatius offered a handshake).  
* **What Players Learned:** The Harmony students view the Ash-Bloods as exotic novelties. They assume the soot/fire is a choice or a costume that can be "wiped off" \[`1159`, `1160`\].

#### **7\. The Intake Attendant (Teal Butler)**

* **Interaction:** Tried to rush **Britt** out of the cubicle.  
* **What Players Learned:** The Academy is focused on "Throughput" and efficiency. They treat candidates like cattle to be processed \[`1146`\].

#### **8\. The Intake Supervisor**

* **Interaction:** Cleaned up **Iggy‚Äôs** slime mess on the receipt machine.  
* **What He Said:** "Welcome to Curiosity."  
* **What Players Learned:** Even the supervisors are overwhelmed by the chaos of the intake. He waved Iggy through despite Iggy not using the receipt correctly \[`1153`\].

#### **9\. The Weeping Giant & The Consoling Guard**

* **Interaction:** **Lomi** witnessed this while walking through the line.  
* **What Was Said:** "Come on, sir. Your test is done. Please don't try it again. No, you can't."  
* **What Players Learned:** The stakes are life-ruining. Failing the exam means being physically dragged away. The guards are sympathetic but firm \[`1149`\].

#### **10\. The Turban Guard**

* **Interaction:** Confronted **Iggy** about the stolen turban/tissue.  
* **What Happened:** Iggy handed back the snot-filled turban. The guard was flabbergasted.  
* **What Players Learned:** Iggy can get away with social chaos because people don't know how to react to him \[`1184`\].

#### **11\. Cassius**

* **Interaction:** **Lomi** approached him at the pit.  
* **What He Said:** "We have it all masked out... optimal flow... but, well, we don't have a source of flame yet."  
* **What Players Learned:** The students are scientifically prepared (airflow mechanics) but lack the "Spark" (Variant Magic) to actually start the fire. This sets up **Ignatius** (or Lomi) to solve the problem \[`1209`\].

### **III. Mentioned / Background (Not yet met)**

* **Captain Elara Thorne:** Mentioned in lore as the one who escorted Lady Ignis \[`1122`\].  
* **The "Paper Man":** Mentioned in Britt/Aggie's backstory as the sterile man who brought the contract \[`1119`\].

# 0Ô∏è‚É£ Session 0

Here is the revised screenplay for **Session 0**, starting with the **Mizizi Clan**.

This version preserves the specific lore details regarding the clan's history, philosophy ("When things stop dying, we start dying"), and the specific nature of their pact with Harmony, as these are critical to the narrative.

---

### **SCENE 1: THE TURTLE-MUSHROOM FATE**

**INT. VIRTUAL TABLETOP \- NIGHT**

**GM (LUKE S)** (Laughing) Yeah, you were a turtle combined with the mushroom. Turtle mushroom thing.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** Literally mine too. I'm telling you there's like‚Äîwe think the same or something.

**JOHN HAGEY (IGNATIUS)** This was fate. This was decided by fate. We're not changing anything.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** You can't fight fate.

**GM (LUKE S)** And you just defined your clan so well... the turtle mushroom folk who live in the swamp.

**(NARRATION)**

**GM (LUKE S)** Your home is inside this huge fossilized mega-flora... somewhere between the Pandora tree and hobbit holes. Your family history is all about one thing: "When things must die." The legends, the lore that you have been taught as a harrowing tale is: **"When things stop dying, we start dying."**

(Beat)

**GM (LUKE S)** It's weird... like a relationship with life and death that's not normal. It's scary when things stop dying. And that's why your clan has been really concerned lately because things *have* started to not die. The forest, which kept you segregated for hundreds of years, failed. The lore often talks about how the purpose of the forest is to keep you apart from the world because when the world comes, things stop dying.

**(FLASHBACK: THE ARRIVAL OF THE PAPER MAN)**

**GM (LUKE S)** Last cycle, or maybe two cycles ago... a group came, led by a man in what seemed to you to be a very sterile outfit. It didn't have any moss growing off of it. It had no holes in it. It was just very bland and had metal on it. Y'all don't wear metal.

**GM (LUKE S)** The man started bringing things that the elders were now distributing to the clan... you became like the fire brigade. You were starting to just try to destroy the forest around you to get it to die. Harmony comes and they seem to take the soil and the roots and the bark and the stone... neither really are you sure what they're looking for. But in return, they're giving you weapons to destroy your home, which is exactly what you want.

**(RETURN TO TABLE)**

**GM (LUKE S)** Now the next generation has come... the Paper Man has offered much more of the Mycelium clan can now join the Vumbua Academy this year, and the two of you elected to join.

---

### **SCENE 2: THE COUSINS**

**INT. VIRTUAL TABLETOP \- CONTINUOUS**

**GM (LUKE S)** (To Sophie) Sophie, your character is maybe a little bit outspoken... uncertain about their relationship with Harmony, maybe even a little suspicious of it. And Kristina (Aggie), maybe you have had some gossip together about Harmony... but she may not be quite as aggressive as you.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** How would we know each other? I feel like our clan's probably not that big, right?

**GM (LUKE S)** Correct. Everyone probably knows everybody.

**AGGIE (VIA LUKE S)** (Relayed thought) I feel like it would be distant relatives... maybe cousins or second cousins. Know enough about each other that when we find out we're going to the same school, it makes sense they would connect.

**LUKE FOREMAN (LOMI)** Same year at Turtle Camp.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** (Excited) What if we're cousins and we're in the same year at school? We've always been sort of forced together... but we obviously are similar in a lot of ways.

**GM (LUKE S)** Like we go to school but we're very different groups... outspoken versus the quiet.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** I'm gonna add to our story here. I'm going to say I've had the same thoughts. We're both sort of in cahoots on like‚Äî**something is wrong**. The call is coming from inside the house. And we're about to go save our families and save all of our people... we have a mission and we're going to do it together.

### **SCENE 3: CIVILIZATION**

**EXT. EDGE OF THE FOREST \- DAY**

**BRITT** (Gray, dusty, powdery fungal-turtle) and **AGGIE** (Red-and-white spotted mushroom-turtle) step out of the petrified woods.

**GM (LUKE S)** You pop out in the edge of the forest... you can see what you can only really define as "civilization" coming. It is a sprawling tower surrounded by huge buildings and all of these moving metal creatures... It is an assault on your senses.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** (Narrating Action) I think my gut reaction would be to grab Kristina. Like my body stiffens and I feel overwhelmed and stunned and I communicate that with you just by reaching out.

**AGGIE (VIA LUKE S)** (Narrating Action) I think my character would be looking for a darker corner or wall... looking for that safe spot. So she kind of grabs back and waddles off to find that safe spot.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** (To Aggie) Are you more turtle or more fungus?

**AGGIE (VIA LUKE S)** Shape-wise turtle... but definitely on the mushroom side. I want the turtle shell to be like the red and white spotted mushroom that you drop into.

**SOPHIE (BRITT)** I'm going to be a similar vibe... but much more gray and sort of dusty, powdery.

**GM (LUKE S)** As you exit this forest, you're close enough to the Ash Bloods' homes that you can see on the horizon the smoke of their perpetual volcano. And the only people out here are the folks who have made arrangements with the Mycelium clan to come and harvest some of the wood... logging is helping kill the forest and then it's just growing right back.
