Here is the continuation of the screenplay for **Session 0**, covering the introductions of the Earthkin, Emberkin, and Lomi, followed by The Trials.

---

### **SCENE 4: THE DOCKS**

**EXT. VUMBUA DOCKS \- DAY**

**THE MOLE (HOLLY)**, a chronically sickly Earthkin made of packed, crumbling dirt, emerges from the water. He wears large goggles over giant bug eyes.

**THE MOLE (HOLLY)** (Mumbling, frantic) I gotta get more sunscreen.

He scrambles to cover himself, injecting pressurized fluid into his goggles to stop them from steaming in the sun. He moves erratically, taking a zigzagging route to absorb information while covering his tracks.

**GM (LUKE S)** (Describing the Scene) I kind of like this idea that when he came up... there was an old man sitting on the side of the wharf... just waddles over and throws a really heavy trench coat on top of you. And it's very heavy and it compresses on your shoulders a little bit.

**THE MOLE (HOLLY)** (Exhales deeply) (Blinks, shooting water out of goggles) ...Contentment as he has weight back on him.

---

### **SCENE 5: THE PILGRIMAGE**

**EXT. THE EMBER TRAIL \- DAY**

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)**, a rebellious Emberkin teenager with a backpack, arrives in the city. He looks at the magitek lights powered by Harmony's crystal batteries.

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** (Internal Monologue) We're subbing out our own fuel for this fake stuff. It's all fake. It's all wrong. It's not how it should be.

**GM (LUKE S)** (Clarifying) To the elders, you were banished to this trial of adventure...

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** (To the Elders, in Flashback) No, this is simply a pilgrimage.

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** (Internal Monologue) I'm going to find the new source of heat for the clan and everything's going to go back to the way it should be.

---

### **SCENE 6: THE BOILER ROOM**

**INT. VUMBUA UNDER-CITY \- BOILER ROOM \- DAY**

**LOMI (LUKE F)** finishes a shift at the furnace. He is a "blue-collar grease monkey," perpetually covered in soot and dirt. He grabs his gear, not bothering to shower, and heads up to the Academy.

**EXT. VUMBUA STREETS \- CONTINUOUS**

Lomi walks toward the Academy. He spots a **RECEPTIONIST** casually shredding a document and tossing it into a bin without looking. Lomi stops.

**LOMI (LUKE F)** Hey, you know, there's people in this city that take care of that stuff. You know, it doesn't just get done.

The Receptionist stares at him.

**LOMI (LUKE F)** Public infrastructure is important and there are people that run this city.

Lomi walks away, muttering. He recalls his family's advice: *"Someone's got to fix the ship if it goes wrong."*

---

### **SCENE 7: THE TRIALS**

**INT. VUMBUA ACADEMY \- GREAT HALL \- DAY**

The group joins 100,000 other candidates.

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating) The application is... you show up to take the trials and that's your application... that's why there's 100,000 people showing up.

**GM (LUKE S)** (Describing the Vibe) "Come be an explorer. The time is now. The world is open." Very 1920s somewhere in between like *Avatar Korra* type world that's just really excited for this opportunity.

**GM (LUKE S)** (Explaining the Mechanics) The trials is what ranks your likelihood of being a successful candidate... it gives you a role, an explorer role... which it basically is going to be your Daggerheart Class.

The players take the assessment (a meta-game survey).

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** This feels like *Ender's Game* style stuff and I love it.

**GM (LUKE S)** (Reviewing Results) I was determined to make it so that it would be really hard to meta the result. It is... super interesting.

**LOMI (LUKE F)** Is it an "Oops, all bards" situation or are we pretty good?

**GM (LUKE S)** No, no, it's actually like... the party is pretty well balanced. Like zero repeat classes.

**BRITT (SOPHIE)** Wow. Even me and Kristina (Aggie) didn't have the same one?

**GM (LUKE S)** No, you guys do not. Not really even close on this one.

**GM (LUKE S)** (Closing the Session) The crew will have a chance at the "Chosen One" storyline. I'll tell you that like... none of you are "Rust," which is the bottom tier.

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** Yo, good work team.

**FADE OUT.**

# Radio Recap(s)

Good evening, citizens of Harmony and dreamers of the Frontier\! This is Sterling Vance, broadcasting live from the gleaming spires of Vumbua Academy. Today marks the Great Intake, where one hundred thousand hopefuls have flooded our gates, seeking not just glory, but survival. The air is electric, the magitek is humming, and we have our eyes on a very specific, very peculiar set of candidates making waves on the intake floor.

Let's start with a twist of destiny that has the registrars buzzing. I‚Äôm looking at two candidates from the Mycelium Clan‚ÄîBritt and Aggie. And would you believe it? Despite coming from the deep Petrifaction Fields, they have arrived with an almost identical aesthetic. I am hearing one of the Ash Blood candidates, Ignatius, shouting it from the crowd right now‚Äîhe is calling it fate\! He is yelling, "This was decided by fate. We're not changing anything." And folks, he is right. They are both Turtle-Mushroom folk\!

Let‚Äôs dig into the background of these two. We are pulling the archives on the Mizizi Clan lore, and it is chilling. Their history is defined by one terrifying truth: "When things stop dying, we start dying." Can you imagine? Living in fossilized mega-flora, terrified that the world has stopped decaying? And it has\! The forest failed to keep them segregated.

We know a "Paper Man" arrived in their village wearing a sterile outfit. He brought weapons. Harmony takes their soil and roots, and in exchange, the clan gets tools to destroy their own home just to help it die. Grim stuff\!

Now, let's look at these cousins. Britt appears "outspoken and kind of aggressive," clearly suspicious of Harmony. Her cousin, Aggie? Skeptical, but quieter. They aren't best friends, but they are forced together. And oh, listen to this whisper from Britt to her cousin‚Äîshe says, "The call is coming from inside the house." They are in cahoots\! They are on a mission to save their families from the conspiracy they believe is rotting Harmony from within\!

Watch them as they approach the city gates. The academy is an assault on the senses. Britt‚Äôs body stiffens. She is overwhelmed. She reaches out and grabs Aggie. And Aggie? She is looking for a "darker corner." She grabs back and waddles off to find a safe spot. Two turtle-mushroom cousins against the world\!

Now, pan your attention to the docks. Something is emerging from the water. It‚Äôs an Earthkin, made of packed, crumbling dirt with giant bug eyes\! He looks "chronically sickly." He is steaming in the sun\! He is frantically injecting fluid into his goggles and zig-zagging to avoid being tracked. He is mumbling to himself, "I gotta get more sunscreen."

But wait‚Äîthere is an old man on the wharf. He isn't shocked. He just walks over and throws a heavy trench coat over the mud-man. The Earthkin exhales, water shoots out of his goggles, and he seems to find "contentment as he has weight back on him." A trench coat to save the day\!

Turning our eyes to the Ember Trail\! Here comes the Emberkin teenager, Ignatius. He is half-obsidian, and he is in a rebellious phase. We are hearing reports that he believes Harmony is providing a "false religion flame." He says, "We‚Äôre subbing out our own fuel for this fake stuff." He was banished for exploring forbidden areas, but he is reframing the narrative\! I am hearing him say it now: "No, this is simply a pilgrimage." He is here to find a real flame. That is a kid with a chip on his shoulder\!

And finally, let‚Äôs go underground. Down to the boiler room. We have Lomi. He is a blue-collar grease monkey, folks. You can‚Äôt tell where the skin ends and the dirt begins. He is finishing a shift and heading straight to the Academy.

Oh, this is good. He‚Äôs walking past a receptionist shredding a document, and Lomi stops. He is scolding them\! He says, "Hey, you know, there's people in this city that take care of that stuff. Public infrastructure is important and there are people that run this city." You tell 'em, Lomi\! The city runs on boilers, not magic\!

Now, the moment of truth. The Trials\! One hundred thousand candidates are taking the psychological assessment. Ignatius says it feels like "Ender's Game style stuff." The results are coming in... the administration is reviewing them. Is it an "Oops, All Bards" situation?

No\! The results are in. The party is pretty well balanced. Like zero repeat classes. I am shocked‚Äîeven the mushroom cousins have different classes\! Ignatius chimes in with a "Yo, good work team."

And there you have it, listeners\! They have survived the cull. They are not "Rust" tier. They are a perfectly balanced crew of misfits ready to save‚Äîor break‚Äîthe world. Lets see how these new candidates fair in their gen-ed classes next time\! This is Sterling Vance, signing off\!

# Good evening, citizens of Harmony and dreamers of the Frontier\!

This is Sterling Vance, broadcasting live from the gleaming galleries of the Sky-Spire.

It has been eighty long, quiet years since a new Node was last integrated‚Äîa lifetime of static maps and dwindling dreams. But now? Fervor is sweeping through Harmony like a solar gale\! Vumbua has weighed anchor and settled into it‚Äôs new home\! From the high cafes of the Sky-Spire to the bustling decks of the Deep-Hull, every citizen is asking: What lies in this new Terra?

We‚Äôve all heard the legends of the Ash-blood domains, where the earth itself pulses with a primal heat that promises to reignite our aging forges\! And what of the Mizizi? Their Node is a miracle that defies every law of the Loom‚Äîa resonance that holds death at bay\! Imagine the medicines, the longevity, the pure vitality we are about to stitch into our Core. What other riches will Captains Aris and Valerius bring back to our hearths? The results of these trials are being crunched by the Loom even as I speak, determining who will be the tip of the spear in this new age of discovery\!"

"Today marks the Great Intake\! One hundred thousand hopefuls have flooded our Anchorage, and the air is electric with the arrival of our newest clan members. Let's start with a twist of destiny that has the registrars buzzing. I‚Äôm looking at two candidates from the Mizizi Clan And would you believe it? Despite coming from the deep Petrifaction Fields, they have arrived with an almost identical turtle-mushroom aesthetic. I am hearing the Ash-blood candidate, Ignatius, shouting it from the crowd right now‚Äîhe is calling it 'Geometric Fate\!' He says they aren't changing a thing, and folks, the Loom seems to agree\!

And speaking of that boisterous Ash-blood \- He‚Äôs half-obsidian and carries a fire that matches his ambition. We‚Äôre hearing he‚Äôs on a personal 'Pilgrimage,' seeking to compare the legendary flames of his ancestors with the magnificent beacons of our own Academy. He‚Äôs looking for the ultimate spark, a quest for truth that defines the very spirit of the Venture\!"

"Now, listeners, I know we spent all of last week‚Äôs broadcast covering our aristocrats and the high-born legacies of the Sterling and Thorne lineages‚Äîbut they aren't the only Harmonians showing up today\! Beyond the gilded names, thousands upon thousands of 'us normal folk' have heard the call of the frontier and flocked to our docks to try their hand at the intake exam.

We‚Äôve got simple peasants off the low-bunks of a transport ship. Just like this one here, wow\! He‚Äôs 50% crumbling sediment and 50% waterlogged, gleaming goggles. Now look at this‚Äîacademy camaraderie in action\! An old man on the wharf‚ÄîI bet he‚Äôs from the class of ‚Äò34‚Äîsaw the little guy steaming in the sun and tossed a heavy, oil-stained trench coat over him\! Hah\! That seems to have done it based on the amount of water that shot out of his goggles. A trench coat to save the day\! Welcome to the sun, kid. You're part of the team now.

And we can't forget those who keep the city running while the rest of us dream. Just here, we‚Äôve got a blue-collar hero, folks‚Äîthe kind of grease monkey who keeps the heart of Vumbua beating. He‚Äôs heading straight from a double shift to the Spire Gates, and he‚Äôs already showing his leadership\! He was spotted scolding a receptionist for improper document disposal, reminding them that *'Public infrastructure is the bedrock of our success.'* Spoken like a man who understands that every bolt and rivet is a testament to Harmony. That's dedication\!"

"But as the steam settles on the intake floor, we must remember that the path of the Pioneer is narrow. While our featured candidates have successfully navigated their preliminary screenings, over twenty-two thousand others have already taken their leave‚Äîfinding their purpose not on the frontier, but in the essential roles of City Maintenance and industrial support. They are the bolts that hold our floorboards together, to be sure\! But for the seventy-seven thousand hopefuls still standing, the real test has only just begun. All our eyes are fixed on rare few who will gain that most lustrous title: Exploranaut.

To earn the rank of Exploranaut is to transcend the ordinary. It is an invitation to the Great Council, a life of unparalleled prestige, and a legacy that will be whispered in the Sky-Spires for centuries. Our featured squad has passed the entry requirements\! They are the pioneers of a new age, a nearly balanced crew ready to map the unknown. Let's see how they and the other candidates fair in Ex-Ed 101 tomorrow morning\!

This is Sterling Vance, signing off. Keep your anchors heavy and your hearts light\!"

# 1Ô∏è‚É£ Session 1

# **Session 1: The Venture & The Vances**

**Theme:** Atlantis meets Treasure Planet. High Polish vs. Grimy Reality. **Core Conflict:** The "Savants" (PCs) vs. The "System" (The Aristocrats).

## **üèóÔ∏è Scene 0: The Intake (The Hangar Pavilion)**

**Atmosphere:** A sea of 100,000 bodies swarming the "Anchorage." The intake takes place within a cavernous, temporary iron-and-canvas vault known as **The Intake Pavilion**. This structure is massive, designed with high, vaulted ceilings that will eventually serve as the main hangars for the Academy's walkers and airships once the "Venture" begins. For now, it is a maze of velvet ropes, brass railings, and thousands of percussive typewriter stations.

**Visuals:** The air is thick with the smell of lamp oil, ozone, and the nervous sweat of 100,000 hopefuls. Above, worker-constructs crawl along the iron rafters, readying the fuel lines and docking clamps that will replace the intake desks in mere days. The noise is a constant, vibrating thrum‚Äîthe rhythmic "clank-clank-clank" of the city being assembled outside, echoing within the hollow iron shell of the Pavilion.

### **The Filtering Mechanic: "The Spire Scan"**

To progress toward the Academy gates, every student must first step into one of the hundreds of **Resonance Booths** lining the Pavilion walls.

* **The Process:** You aren't asked your name. You step into the booth, and a brass ring descends over you, humming with teal energy.  
* **The Psychology:** As the ring passes your heart, the Loom triggers a "Micro-Dissolve." For one second, your body feels like it‚Äôs made of static.  
* **The "Rust" Result:** If a student's heart rate spikes too high, or their "Aura" flickers into grey-static, the booth emits a low, mournful foghorn blast.  
  * *The Guard:* "Candidate 88,210. Standing: RUST. Access Denied. Return to the transport for City Maintenance reassignment."  
  * *The Statistics:* \~22,419 candidates (20% of the intake) fail here. Their adventure ends at the very first gate.

### **The Player Intake (The Receipt)**

As the PCs pass their scans, they are directed to heavy iron desks bolted to the floor. On each sits an antiquated, 1920s-style typewriter with brass keys.

* **The Input:** They type their profiles into the lead-heavy keys. As they finish, a small, high-speed machine next to the typewriter chugs out a narrow, stiff strip of parchment‚Äîtheir **Loom Receipt**. This is their only proof of existence within the Academy.  
* **Britt & Iggy:** The receipt is printed on gold-flecked paper. The printer hums a melodic sequence. (100 pts)  
* **Aggie & Ignatius:** The receipt is standard white parchment, crisp and sharp. The printer jitters with a questioning click-clack. (80 pts)  
* **Loami:** The receipt is a rough, industrial-grade grey paper. The typewriter keys clunk like lead under his fingers, and the machine groans as it stamps his score. (50 pts)

### **The Gates (The Gilded Sentinels)**

To exit the Pavilion and enter the Academy proper, students must present their receipts to the **Harmony Wardens** guarding the massive brass-bound Spire Gates.

* **The Guards:** These sentinels have a distinct "Harmony-Sultan" vibe. They wear high-collared tunics of deep teal and white silk, overlaid with polished brass geometric breastplates. Their heads are adorned with high-crested, silk-wrapped helmets, and they hold long-poled "Vibration Halberds" that hum with the same teal energy as the gates. They move with statue-like, percussive discipline.  
* **The Interaction:** The guard takes the receipt, slides it into a brass reader on their belt, and if the light turns green, they strike the floor with their halberd, allowing the candidate to pass.

### **The First View: The Dual-Spire Anchorage**

As the PCs step through the gates, the iron bars swing open to reveal a sprawling garden courtyard‚Äîa pristine Oxford quadrangle that ends at a massive ocean cliffside.

* **The Twin Pillars of Harmony:** Flanking the central path are two titanic vessels docked on stone promontories. On the left, a gilded, vertical airship (**The Sky-Spire**) looms like a golden needle. On the right, a massive, black-hulled steam ship (**The Deep-Hull**) sits low in the water.  
* **The University Core:** Between the two ships, a magnificent stone university hall with gothic arches and stained glass rises up. It is a world of marble, brass piping, and glowing teal conduits.  
* **The Spire-Scape:** Beyond the garden, the air is filled with the skeletons of future buildings. Massive steam cranes and scaffolding towers climb toward the sky, hoisting entire prefabricated classroom wings into place with a thunderous *clack*.

# üèõÔ∏è Scene 1: The Grand Assembly (The Indoctrination)

**Location:** The Oculus Auditorium (located within the Sky-Spire Core). A masterpiece of brass lattice and curved glass overlooking the uncharted clouds of Terra. Thousands of students are packed into vertical galleries, looking down at a small, illuminated stage.

**The "Lie":** Dean Isolde Vane steps to the podium in a crisp, high-collared white uniform. Her voice is amplified by floating brass "Whisper-Cones."

### **The Speech: "The New Horizon"**

"Citizens. Candidates. Look around you. You stand within a legacy built on the courage of those who dared to see the invisible. We are the inheritors of the Great Discovery‚Äîof noble houses like Sterling, Thorne, and Vance, who brought their unique energies into our Core, stitching together the very ground we walk upon for the benefit of all.

For eighty years, our maps have remained static. We have missed the thrill of the unknown, the wonder of meeting new peoples, and the vitality that comes from integrating new spirits into our Harmony. But that silence is over\! For the first time in nearly a century, a new frontier has been revealed\!

We welcome the Ash-bloods, whose mastery of heat brings a new fire to our Core. And we look with awe toward the Mizizi, whose Node boggles even our greatest minds‚Äîa resonance that holds death at bay\! Imagine the medicines, the longevity, the pure vitality we are about to stitch into our Core.

We are honored today by the presence of Captains Aris and Valerius, who charted these lands, and the diplomatic teams who have brought these peoples‚Äîofficially, I am proud to announce‚Äîinto the light of Harmony. Indeed, a Mizizi has already achieved the rank of Exploranaut and represents their lands at the Harmony Seat on our Great Council\!

Today, you follow in those footsteps. You are the needle. You are the thread. Go forth and find the glory that awaits us all\!"

* **The Insight:** (DC 15\) The Dean‚Äôs performance is flawless, but her hand grips the podium so hard the brass creaks. While the speech is a masterpiece of inspiration, there is a sense that the administration needs this class to succeed far more than they are admitting. The talk of "new energy" feels less like a choice and more like a desperate necessity.

# üß¨ Scene 2: Logistics & Dorm Assignments (The "Meat Grinder")

**The Chaos:** Following the speech, the "Sultan-Guard" Wardens use their vibration halberds to herd the 77,000 remaining students toward the **Modular District**. It is a stampede of brass trunks, shouting, and confusion.

### **The Assignment Interface**

At the gate of each dormitory block, a **Loom Kiosk** (typewriter/printer combo) is bolted to the stone.

* **Mechanic:** Students slide their Loom Receipt into a slot. The machine clatters, stamps the parchment, and spits out a brass key-tag.  
* **The Result:** The Loom assigns living quarters based on clannish resonance and nomenclature (Alphabetical). Squad pairing is deferred until after the first academic evaluation.

### **The Dorms**

* **Britt & Aggie (Block 04-Root):** A high-humidity modular unit built into a terraced cliff. The walls are covered in moss-textured insulation, and it smells faintly of damp earth.  
* **Iggy & Ignatius (Block 12-Basalt):** A low-humidity, high-thermal block. Because their names both start with "I," the Loom has bunked the Earthkin and the Ash-blood together. The room is hot, dry, and smells like a forge.  
* **Loami (Block 99-Piston):** Located in the "Industrial Overflow" wing near the Walker-Core. It‚Äôs a loud, vibrating space made of bare iron.

### **The Roommates (Block 99-Piston)**

Since Loami is separated from the others, he finds himself bunking with two "Technical Track" NPCs:

* **"Ratchet":** A Copper-rank cynic who has a prosthetic brass hand. He‚Äôs already taking apart a desk. *"Welcome to the boiler room, kid. Don't believe the Dean. This place isn't a school; it's a battery, and we're the acid."*  
* **"Soot":** A wide-eyed Rust-leaning student who is terrified of being "culled." He treats Loami like an expert because Loami actually knows how a wrench works.

### **The Guide: Celia Vance**

Celia acts as a floating "Compliance Proctor" for the high-variance wing. She appears in the doorways of the various blocks, checking logs.

* *"Celia:* "Candidates, the Loom has determined your current housing is optimal for stabilizing your base frequencies. Do not fraternize across blocks until the first bell. I've already filed three demerits for noise in Block 12\. Try to be... quieter."

# üåÉScene 3: Nighttime Sandbox (The Spire-Scape)

**Theme:** Atlantis meets Treasure Planet. High Polish vs. Grimy Reality. **Context:** Post-Intake. The Squad is formed (alphabetically) but not yet tested.

## **üß¨ Previous Context: Logistics & Dorms (Scene 2\)**

**The Dorms (Home Base):**

* **Britt & Aggie (Block 04-Root):** High-humidity, moss-insulated cliffside unit.  
* **Iggy & Ignatius (Block 12-Basalt):** High-thermal block. Hot, dry, smells of forge.  
* **Loami (Block 99-Piston):** Industrial Overflow. Loud vibrations. Roommates: **Ratchet** (Cynic) & **Soot** (Anxious).

## **üåÖ Establishing Shot: The Golden Hour (Afternoon Free-Roam)**

**The Transition:** As the dorm assignments conclude, a massive, resonant **Steam-Whistle** blows from the Walker-Core, signaling the end of the "Construction Shift."

* **Visuals:** The sun begins to dip below the horizon of the new Terra, casting long, bruised purple shadows across the red rocks. For a moment, the entire Academy catches the light‚Äîthe brass of the **Sky-Spire** flares blindingly gold, while the iron of the **Deep-Hull** turns a deep, cooling blue.  
* **The Shift Change:** The deafening *clank-clank-clank* of the steam cranes slows to a halt. The dust settles. In its place, the hum of the city takes over. Thousands of **Teal Magitek Lanterns** flicker to life along the scaffolded walkways, creating a floating constellation of lights against the darkening sky.  
* **Atmosphere:** The air changes from the smell of ozone and sweat to the scent of roasting meats, spiced cider, and exotic street food carted in by "Normals" hoping to make a coin off the hungry students. The tension of the intake breaks; the "Spire-Scape" transforms from a construction site into a bustling, neon-lit university town.

**GM Read-Aloud:** "The great pistons of the Walker-Core heave a final, exhausted sigh, venting a cloud of white steam that rolls through the streets like fog. The construction noise dies, replaced by music‚Äîlutes from the high balconies, drums from the lower decks. The streetlamps hum to life, painting the brass walkways in electric teal. You have survived the Intake. The night is yours."

### **üìç 1\. The Common Areas (The Central Quad)**

**Vibe:** A festival of survivors.

* **Activity:** A massive bonfire. Harmony officials have provided "Safe-Flame" (a chemically stabilized fuel), but several Ash-blood students are gathered in a smaller circle, trying to summon a "True Spark."  
* **The Hook:** **Sarge (Squad 09\)** sits on a crate, his face a map of old burn scars. He‚Äôs meticulously cleaning a rusted bayonet.  
* **NPC Depth:**  
  * **Backstory:** A non-graduate scout who lost his entire squad to an "Ether-Leak" three years ago. He blamed the leadership and now must graduate to change their chances.  
  * **Bond:** His current "Expendable" squad. He feels a crushing, quiet responsibility for their survival.  
  * **Flaw:** Fatalism. He believes everyone is destined to "dissolve" eventually.  
  * **Motive:** To prevent more youngens from dying.  
* **Interaction:** If Ignatius approaches, Sarge notes the "Pure Obsidian" of his skin. *"You're the one from the Pilgrimage, right? Be careful with that fire, boy. Harmony doesn't like things they can't put out with a switch."*  
* **DM Tip:** Emphasize the visual contrast. The "Safe-Flame" casts no shadows, while the "True Spark" makes shadows dance. This subtle wrongness of Harmony tech is a key theme.  
* **Campaign Tie-In:** Sarge‚Äôs bayonet is made of "Pre-Stitch" steel. If asked, he mutters it's from a "Lost Node." This hints that Harmony has lost territory before, foreshadowing the "Dissolved Lands" they will visit later.

### **üìç 2\. Academy Welcome Events (The Great Hall)**

**Vibe:** Boring official PR mixed with desperate hunger.

* **Activity:** A lecture titled *"The Ethics of Integration"* plays on loop. Most students are ignoring it in favor of the free cider and hard tack.  
* **The Hook:** **Lucky (Squad 09\)** is working the room. He‚Äôs wearing a stolen Gold-rank sash and telling a group of terrified Copper students that he can "influence the Loom" for the price of their dessert rations.  
* **NPC Depth:**  
  * **Backstory:** A street urchin from the Anchorage outskirts who pickpocketed a dead candidate's Loom Receipt to get into the intake.  
  * **Bond:** A younger sister living in the "Low-Bunks" whom he sends his extra rations to.  
  * **Flaw:** Pathological Grifter. He cannot stop the "hustle," even when it‚Äôs counter-productive.  
  * **Motive:** To "fake it 'til he makes it" into a comfortable administrative job where he doesn't have to bleed.  
* **Interaction:** If Loami catches him, Lucky doesn't panic. He winks. *"Hey, big man. You look like you know how the pipes work. You want in on the best bunk in the Deep-Hull? I just need a 'maintenance override' on Block 12."*  
* **DM Tip:** Lucky isn't just a grifter; he knows the maintenance tunnels better than the faculty. If the players befriend him here, he becomes a crucial contact for smuggling contraband (or people) later in the season.  
* **Campaign Tie-In:** The lecture glosses over "The Silent Era" (the 80-year gap in discovery). A successful History check reveals a gap in the timeline that the Dean is actively hiding.

### **üìç 3\. Private Clubs (The Gilded Balconies)**

**Vibe:** High-society exclusion. Smells of lavender and money.

* **Activity:** The Sterling and Thorne families are hosting an "Aurum Mixer." The air smells of lavender and ozone.  
* **The Hook:** **Valerius Sterling (Squad 01\)** stands on the railing, looking down at the quad. Beside him, **Seraphina Vox** is using a crystal prism to "score" the resonance of students walking below.  
* **NPC Depth (Valerius):**  
  * **Backstory:** Scion of the Sterling family, groomed to lead the Venture. He has never actually touched dirt; his hands are magically calloused to look "rugged."  
  * **Bond:** The Sterling family reputation‚Äîhe carries it like a heavy, gilded shield.  
  * **Flaw:** Narcissism. He cannot process the idea of someone being more "efficient" than him.  
  * **Motive:** To find a Node so massive it secures his father's seat on the High Council forever.  
* **NPC Depth (Seraphina):**  
  * **Backstory:** A musical prodigy who views the world as a symphony. She finds Harmony's industrial noises "physically painful."  
  * **Bond:** Her "Harmonic Tuning" kit; she treats the delicate crystal forks like children.  
  * **Flaw:** Aesthetic Elitism. She literally gets a migraine from "ugly" or "low-frequency" people.  
  * **Motive:** To record the "Primal Song" of a Shattered Node and ascend to Grand Maestro.  
* **Interaction:** Valerius spots Britt and Aggie. *"Look, Seraphina. The Loom is desperate. They're letting the Mycelium waddle into our auditoriums. I suppose even a garden needs fertilizer."* Seraphina laughs, a sound like glass breaking. *"Their aesthetic is... dissonant, Val. It hurts my eyes to even chart them."*  
* **DM Tip:** Getting into this area requires a disguise (Britt/Iggy) or a servant's uniform (Loami). It's a social stealth challenge.  
* **Campaign Tie-In:** If Aggie gets close, Seraphina's tuning fork reacts unexpectedly‚Äîhumming a "perfect 5th" instead of dissonance. Seraphina looks confused. This hints that the Mizizi biology is naturally more "Harmonious" than the Academy admits, a key plot point for the Mizizi Node arc.

### **üìç 4\. Clan Assistance & Integration (The Help Desk)**

**Vibe:** Overworked and underfunded.

* **Activity:** A small, overworked booth. A Mizizi student named **Kojo** is trying to explain "Geometric Syntax" to a group of confused Earthkin.  
* **The Hook:** **Pudge (Squad 09\)** is hovering near the back. He isn't there for the math; he‚Äôs realized the Mizizi bring "Life-Capsules" (concentrated nutrients) that Harmony doesn't track as food.  
* **NPC Depth (Pudge):**  
  * **Backstory:** Son of a farmer whose land was "stitched" into a industrial zone. He‚Äôs been hungry since he was six years old.  
  * **Bond:** His mother‚Äôs copper cooking spoon, which he carries in his boot.  
  * **Flaw:** Cowardice. He will betray almost anyone for a hot meal.  
  * **Motive:** To find a world with enough food that nobody ever has to fight for it.  
* **Interaction:** Pudge whispers to Aggie. *"You got any more of those 'Root-Chews'? I'll swap you a brass-knuckle for a handful. I'm literally starving. This 'Rust' ration is just sawdust and water."*  
* **DM Tip:** Kojo is overwhelmed. Helping him (Intellect check) earns a "Mizizi Translation Codex" item (useful for exams).  
* **Campaign Tie-In:** The "Life-Capsules" Pudge is stealing are actually dormant seeds. If planted, they grow instant cover. This serves as a tutorial on Mizizi bio-tech for the players.

### **üìç 5\. The Great Library (The Forbidden Wing)**

**Vibe:** Silent, cold, and tense.

* **Activity:** Students are researching for the first exam. The air is deathly silent.  
* **The Hook:** A tall, gaunt Ash-blood scholar named **Pyrrhus** with white-hot eyes is arguing with a Librarian. He‚Äôs pointing to a map of the "Shattered Node Variant."  
* **NPC Depth:**  
  * **Backstory:** An ex-priest of the Emberkin who was banished for "Heresy" when he claimed the Ancestors were screaming for help.  
  * **Bond:** The "Living Flame" he carries in a specialized lantern‚Äîhe says it's his father's soul.  
  * **Flaw:** Paranoia. He believes every Harmony official is trying to "snuff out" his light.  
  * **Motive:** To find the source of the heat-drain and stop Vumbua from "choking" the world.  
* **Interaction:** If Ignatius listens (Perception DC 14), Pyrrhus is frantic. *"The heat isn't fading\! It's being diverted\! Look at the ley-lines‚Äîthey don't feed the city, they feed the Spire\!"* The Librarian signals two Wardens to escort him out.  
* **DM Tip:** The Librarian is a Construct who only responds to absolute silence. Speaking triggers a "Shushing Beam" (minor psychic damage).  
* **Campaign Tie-In:** Pyrrhus drops a map fragment when escorted out. It shows a "Heat Sink" located directly under the Dean‚Äôs office. This is a direct clue to the "Minimum" crisis and a potential mid-campaign heist location.

### **üìç 6\. Sky-Spire Auditoriums (The Observation Deck)**

**Vibe:** Awe-inspiring views and military strategy.

* **Activity:** The massive telescopes are unlocked. Students can see the swirling, purple-and-teal chaos of the Terra below.  
* **The Hook:** **Cassius Thorne (Squad 01\)** is lecturing a group of subordinates on "Surgical Strike" points.  
* **NPC Depth:**  
  * **Backstory:** His grandfather was the General who "suppressed" the Ash-blood Uprising 30 years ago. He wants to finish the job.  
  * **Bond:** The Thorne Legion code‚Äîa black iron signet ring he never takes off.  
  * **Flaw:** Bloodlust. He views every interaction as a tactical encounter to be won or lost.  
  * **Motive:** To militarize the Venture and turn the new frontier into a Thorne protectorate.  
* **Interaction:** He makes eye-contact with Iggy. *"You Earthkin... you're dense. Good. When the drop-pods hit the crust, I'll need someone heavy to soak up the impact. Try not to crumble before the first week is out."*  
* **DM Tip:** Describe the "Shattered Nodes" below not as land, but as floating islands drifting apart. This reinforces the urgency of the "Stitching."  
* **Campaign Tie-In:** Cassius is marking "Bombardment Zones." One of them is the village where the players will likely go in Session 3\. This sets up the inevitable conflict between the players (explorers) and Squad 01 (conquerors).

### **üìç 7\. Deep-Hull Decks (The Vents)**

**Vibe:** The underground gambling ring. Hot and greasy.

* **Activity:** Below the lecture halls, the "Real Academy" happens. Students are gambling on the outcome of the first exam.  
* **The Hook:** A group of older students (Year 3\) are taking bets on which Squad 7 variant will "Dissolve" first.  
* **Interaction:** Loami hears his name mentioned. *"5-to-1 on the Alpha-7 cluster. They've got the Mizizi cousins and the 'Trench-coat' Earthkin. That squad's a suicide pact waiting to happen."*  
* **DM Tip:** The gambling currency is "Chits" (Battery Charge). Players can actually wager here to gain starting resources, but losing means starting the exam with a disadvantage.  
* **Campaign Tie-In:** The betting book has a list of "Previous Squads." Almost all of them are crossed out. This reinforces the lethality of the job and gives Loami a tangible list of "Ghost Squads" to investigate later.

## **üìÖ Scene 4: The Speed-Run (The First Week)**

* **Monday:** "Cartography & The Lie of the Horizon."  
* **Tuesday:** "Harmonic Ethics: Why the Manual is Always Right."  
* **Wednesday:** "Practical Anchor Maintenance." (Loami shines).  
* **Thursday:** "Xenobiology: What to Kill and What to Stitch."  
* **Friday:** "The Calculus of Sacrifice."

## **üìù Scene 5: The First Exam (The Gauntlet)**

* **The Setup:** 77,000 students in **Simulation Pods**.  
* **The Stakes:** Top 1,000 to Sky-Spire; Bottom 20,000 Rusted out.  
* **Action:** Transition players to **Venture\_Exam\_Survey.md**.

### **End of Session 1\.**

# Script 1

This is a great note. You are right; the specific flavor of the "Teal Butlers" and the mechanics of the typewriter add so much texture to the setting.

Here is the **Revised Part 1**, restoring the GM‚Äôs descriptive text and the specific interactions with the "Rust" rejection and the Supervisor.

---

### **SCENE 1: THE INTAKE EXAM**

**INT. INTAKE PAVILION \- CUBICLES \- DAY**

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating) So, the machine in front of you prints out that first question... all the way up until "Begin Intake." You didn't have to know how to use the typewriter. You just look down and say, "Okay, question number four is four." *Click.* Number three is three. *Click.*

(Beat) It prints out the rank... Gold, Silver, Copper, Rust. It cuts itself off and drops into your hand. A little flag pings up on the corner‚Äî*Ping\! Ping\!*‚Äîand suddenly an attendant is there to whisk you away. These attendants are running around in these teal butler ties... sort of somewhere between a Sultan and an English butler.

**GM (LUKE S)** (To Sophie) Britt, you would have finished your survey first. If you wanted to try to stall for Aggie to finish her test, you can. Otherwise, y'all are going to get pulled apart in the current.

**BRITT (SOPHIE)** I think I try to stall. Yeah. As I finish, the little flag automatically goes ding. Can I grab the flag and just like... hold it back down?

**GM (LUKE S)** (Describing the consequence) I think that you were able to get it down. But you can see someone... it's like the airport traffic guard. He's way down there on a point and he's walking to you. You can tell that you're going to be the next car that gets the whistle blown at you.

**BRITT (SOPHIE)** Can I try to rip my ticket off and shove it in my pocket and be like... "Something happened\! It didn't print\! Like the Bluetooth's not connected\!"

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Attendant) "You finished your exam. Okay, this way, please come."

**BRITT (SOPHIE)** "No, it didn't print. It didn't print. Let me... I'm going to look under the table." (Action) I just get down and start looking underneath. Just shuffling around underneath the desk.

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Attendant) "Excuse me, ma'am. It really is time to go. This cubicle needs to be cleared for the next candidate."

**BRITT (SOPHIE)** "It didn't print\!" (Action) I think I stand up and my shell hits the desk and it knocks over the typewriter. Then I pull it out of my pocket and I say, "Oh, I found it."

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Attendant) "Please... please follow me, ma'am."

**BRITT (SOPHIE)** I think I make eye contact with Aggie and I follow.

---

### **SCENE 2: THE WORKING MAN & THE CULL**

**INT. INTAKE PAVILION \- HALLWAY \- CONTINUOUS**

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating) As you are working your way through, about one in five is being pulled in a different direction than you. Their flags went up... but the attendants aren't checking receipts until the end. It's like Costco‚Äîthere‚Äôs two guys with a Sharpie checking it off. They are soldier types, wearing thicker jerkens wrapped in an intricate pattern.

**LOMI (LUKE F)** I think just during the general stroll... Lomi's talking with the guy. (In Character) "Hey, there's quite a lot of you here. How's your benefits? You all right? Everybody doing well? They paying you well here?"

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Attendant) "You are a Copper. It is always good to know your options. I hope you make it through the next round. Do you need a job?"

**LOMI (LUKE F)** "Ah, no. I got a life calling in the boiler room. Family born and raised. Boiler mega-union."

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating the background action) "Come on, sir. Your test is done. Please don't try it again. No, you can't. I'm sorry." (Narrating) You see a different colored attendant, slightly more bulky, come and grab a guy. The guy is just weeping as he gets pulled to the side. The attendant looks back at Lomi. (As Attendant) "Oh, sorry about that. Um... you're talking about boiling water?"

**LOMI (LUKE F)** "Yeah, you know, you are doing great work here and you keep doing your thing. I see you're very busy. Just want to make sure you're being taken care of."

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating) He ducks as someone throws a hat off the tin. (As Attendant) "Oh gosh, um... thank you for your concern. If you have a God, please pray."

---

### **SCENE 3: IGGY'S CHAOS**

**INT. INTAKE PAVILION \- IGGY'S CUBICLE \- CONTINUOUS**

**IGGY (HOLLY)** I think Iggy is gonna ask... (In Character) "Sir... do you have a tissue? I could use a tissue."

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Attendant) "No."

**IGGY (HOLLY)** "That's okay. That's okay. I have an idea." (Action) He goes up to the receipt thing that's been printing and he just pulls down.

**GM (LUKE S)** Oh, no.

**IGGY (HOLLY)** "I got it. I got it. I have one more question. Where am I?"

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Attendant) "Oh god. That just dropped our throughput by 100 candidates. This is terrible." (As Supervisor) A taller figure starts working their way through the con. "Oh, um... that's my supervisor. Can you help me fix it? No, it's already gross. Oh, it's so gross." (Narrating) He's picking up slime off of the receipt generator.

**IGGY (HOLLY)** "But I don't know what this is."

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Supervisor) "Does Iggy use his receipt at all?"

**IGGY (HOLLY)** No, no, he did not use his receipt.

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Supervisor) He waves and grabs Iggy by the arm. "Sir, this way towards the entrance. Welcome to Vumbua."

**IGGY (HOLLY)** "Well, thank you so much. I do have questions."

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Supervisor) "Good, good. That's what you're here for. Welcome to Curiosity."

---

### **SCENE 4: THE COURTYARD REVEAL**

**EXT. VUMBUA COURTYARD \- DAY**

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating) You come through these large marble pillars into this huge courtyard. A monstrous ironclad cruise ship with brass fittings sits in a harbor. Next to it is a smaller version of it that has this airship balloon tied to it. The people are just so small compared to these vessels.

**GM (LUKE S)** (To John) Ignatius, you want to roll me something to see how the hell you're processing here? Because I don't think he's seen anything like this.

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** (Rolling) I think that... nine with Fear.

**GM (LUKE S)** Nine with Fear. I think Ignatius... there's kind of a lot going on here.

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** I think Ignatius had this facade of confidence walking in and getting through this, it just melts away. Like, "What the f\*\*\*?"

**GM (LUKE S)** (As "Chad" Student) Coming right after you is a tall, nicely dressed, kind of Bridgerton-esque vibe but a little more meat on him. "Don't worry, Chad. It's so... welcome to the show, mate. Oh, wait, are you... from the Ashland Islands? The Ember Isles?"

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** "What gave it away? Was it the soot or the literal flames?"

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Chad) "Um, you are on fire, lad. Yes, it's back, right?" (Beat) "It's hard to wipe off. I mean, it's something that never leaves you. I... all respect. I hope not, actually. I'll see you." (Walking away, then turning) "Oh... will your hand burn me?"

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** "I don't think so." (Action) I shake his hand.

**GM (LUKE S)** It doesn't burn him. (As Chad) "Alright, jolly good." (Narrating) He storms off, spitting and trying to get the soot off his hand.

**IGNATIUS (JOHN)** I think Ignatius finds this really funny because like... that's not a normal thing for him to always be covered in soot. It's just because of how far he's traveled. He plays into it every now and then. We're not barbarians. We clean ourselves.

---

### **SCENE 5: THE UNION MAN**

**EXT. VUMBUA COURTYARD \- CONSTRUCTION ZONE \- CONTINUOUS**

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating) Lomi, you might have even seen some of the inside of Vumbua because you came across as part of the maintenance crew. It wouldn't be a huge surprise to you. But I think you're maybe a little bit proud? It is getting pretty close to holding students and it was just a boat and a ship like half a year ago.

**LOMI (LUKE F)** (Previously "Loami or Britt") I think he he's coming out and just looking around and going... (In Character) "Yeah, this will do. They do good work. You know? What can we say? It's a little more cushy than the Boiler Room. I'll say it. Doesn't take as much grit... but they do good work."

**GM (LUKE S)** (Narrating) Lomi, you recognize someone. There is someone else who surprises you coming out of the exams. All you know him by is **Sarge**. You know him because the workers would have these campfires set up... the social hour. (As Sarge) He catches your eye. "Loaves? Loaves, we made it. Can you believe it?"

**LOMI (LUKE F)** "Hey, Sarge\! You made it in\! Hey, I was feeling pretty good about myself until I saw *you* come in, huh? They let anyone in here, huh?"

**LOMI (LUKE F)** "You always guess C, right? That's what they say."

**GM (LUKE S)** (As Sarge) "Is that the third one? Yeah. I just looked at the typewriter. Seems about right. S\*\*\*, dude. It's kind of a lot going on. I don't know if I'm actually cut out for this."
